### 89E — Dry-Run Simulation UX Refinement and Operator Guidance (2026-06-28)

Refined human-readable dry-run output with structured sections per decision type:
SIMULATED BLOCK (Type/Override/Governed alternative), SIMULATED DENY (PERMANENT),
SIMULATED REVIEW REQUIRED (GATE distinction, redaction warning), SIMULATED ALLOW
(explicit non-authorization note), SIMULATED REQUIREMENT, and SIMULATED EVIDENCE
REQUIRED. Fixed next-action wording (pcae dry-run explain, not advisory explain).
Enhanced footer as active "PCAE did NOT" checklist. Source changed: _print_human_readable
refactored into 7 focused helper functions. JSON schema, all safety invariants,
and full test suite preserved. Fast-green: 3,221/26.67s. Full suite: 9,311 pass.
Delivers `docs/PHASE_89_DRY_RUN_BLOCKING_SIMULATION_UX_REFINEMENT.md`. Recommends 89F.

### 89D — Dry-Run Simulation Test Matrix and CLI Stability Review (2026-06-28)

Expanded dry-run simulation test matrix from 74 to 244 tests (+170) plus 24 CLI
subprocess tests across 8 categories: read-only allow (14), hard-block (7),
shell embedded (8), env-prefix (5), compact operator (8), redaction (8),
explain/status (4), and JSON stability (7). Added cross-cutting safety invariant
verification across 12 command types. CLI exit codes verified (0=allow, 1=blocked).
Human-readable and JSON output stability reviewed. All 19 simulation decisions
explainable with severity and enforcement readiness. 3 deferred defects (echo
$VAR, cat .env, sudo prefix). No source fixes needed. Fast-green: 3,221/26s.
Full suite: 9,311 passed, zero failures. Delivers
`docs/PHASE_89_DRY_RUN_BLOCKING_SIMULATION_TEST_MATRIX.md`. Recommends 89E.

### 89C — Dry-Run Blocking Simulation Prototype (2026-06-28)

Implemented `pcae dry-run check/explain/status` as designed in 89B. New
`src/pcae/core/dry_run.py` wraps advisory/broker/shell-gate evidence in a
simulation envelope with simulation_id, severity (info/caution/review_required/
blocked/unknown), enforcement readiness, governed alternatives, and safety
invariants. `src/pcae/commands/dry_run.py` provides CLI with human-readable
output (SIMULATED BLOCK/REVIEW REQUIRED banners, footer) and JSON mode.
Differentiated exit codes: 0=allow, 1=blocked/deny. Registered in cli.py as
`pcae dry-run` group. 74 fast-green tests covering envelope structure,
invariant fields, decision mapping, severity, hard-block preservation,
secret redaction, explain, status, and compound commands. All 11 authorization/
enforcement/interception fields unconditionally false. Fast-green: 3,075/24.87s.
Delivers `docs/PHASE_89_DRY_RUN_BLOCKING_SIMULATION_PROTOTYPE.md`. Recommends 89D.

### 89B — Dry-Run Blocking Simulation Design (2026-06-28)

Design-only phase. Defines PCAE's dry-run blocking simulation layer — the bridge
between advisory mode (Stage 1) and blocking enforcement (Stage 3). Recommends
`pcae dry-run check` command namespace. Covers simulation decision vocabulary
(19 values), JSON output model (50+ fields), human-readable output model with
SIMULATED prefix, severity/recommendation models, hard-block/human-review/
missing-evidence/secret-redaction simulation behavior, accepted-risk and
human-approval boundaries, 16 safety invariants, failure modes, and implementation
roadmap (89C→89G+). Future test matrix: ~250 tests. Records 3 known full-suite
baseline failures from 89A. Delivers
`docs/PHASE_89_DRY_RUN_BLOCKING_SIMULATION_DESIGN.md`. Recommends 89C.

### 89A — Advisory Mode Hardening / False-Positive Repair (2026-06-28)

Fixed 3 known false positives and 1 false negative from 88Y. Added known
shells list (bash, sh, zsh, dash, fish, ksh, tcsh, csh) so shell programs
are recognized and require human review rather than blocked as unknown.
Shell -c/-lc flags now extract and classify embedded commands directly,
preserving hard blocks (sh -c 'git push' → raw_git_push). Compact operator
regex splitting (\|\||&&|;|\|) handles operators without surrounding spaces,
fixing env|grep TOKEN false negative (now properly split as pipe chain and
redacted). env argument inspection differentiates program execution (env python)
from secret variable assignment (env OPENAI_API_KEY=x cmd), fixing the
88V.1 env/printenv over-classification. All 88V.1 secret redaction rules and
hard-block decisions preserved. 1,054 focused tests pass; fast-green unchanged
at ~3,001/~25s. Delivers
`docs/PHASE_89_ADVISORY_MODE_HARDENING_FALSE_POSITIVE_REPAIR.md`. Recommends 89B.

### 88Z — Advisory Operator UX and Workflow Design (2026-06-28)

Design-only phase. Defines the operator-facing UX for PCAE advisory mode:
how human operators read, trust, triage, explain, and act on advisory decisions.
Covers five operator personas, three operator workflows, ten UX principles,
five severity levels, fifteen operator actions, hard-block/human-review/
missing-evidence/secret-redaction/advisory-only messaging design, false-positive
and false-negative handling workflows, operator next-action decision tree,
safety invariants, and a future implementation plan mapped across 89A–89F+.
No implementation — all design. Records known lifecycle issue: PCAE lacks a
governed "final task close to idle" path (pcae check/commit hooks require an
active task contract). Delivers
`docs/PHASE_88_ADVISORY_OPERATOR_UX_AND_WORKFLOW_DESIGN.md`. Recommends 89A.

### 88Y.5 — Project State Shared Evidence Optimization (2026-06-27)

Performance optimization. Extended the shared evidence model from 88Y.3/88Y.4
to the five upstream build functions by adding an optional `ctx=None` parameter
to `build_memory_snapshot`, `build_governance_timeline`, `build_decision_log`,
`build_risk_register`, and `build_project_state`. Updated `GateDryRunContext`
property methods to pass `ctx=self`, so each build function is called exactly
once per gate dry-run invocation instead of repeatedly through the cascade.
Key finding: `build_governance_timeline`, `build_decision_log`, and
`build_risk_register` each called their upstream build functions but never used
the returned values — these vestigial calls are skipped entirely when ctx is
provided. Also eliminates 4 redundant git subprocess calls inside
`build_project_state` by deriving git data from ctx properties. Per-call runtime
reduced from 9.16s to 3.22s (-65%); cumulative reduction from original 88Y.2
baseline: 20.86s → 3.22s (-85%). Added 24 tests in `test_project_state_context.py`
covering decision equivalence (8), memoization (7), freshness (2),
no-persistence (2), backward compatibility (4), idempotency (1). Fixed one test
in `test_gate_dry_run_context.py` tracking function to accept `ctx` kwarg.
No gate decisions, output schema, or governance rules changed. No persistent
cache, no global cache, no cross-invocation cache. Doc at
`docs/PHASE_88_PROJECT_STATE_SHARED_EVIDENCE_OPTIMIZATION.md`. Next: 88Z.

### 88Y.4 — Gate Dry-Run Decision Equivalence and Performance Matrix (2026-06-27)

Validation and hardening phase. Fixed None-sentinel memoization bug in
`GateDryRunContext` — properties returning `None` (task_contract, git_porcelain,
git_branch, git_ahead_count) were recomputed on every access because `None`
doubled as the "not yet computed" sentinel. Introduced `_UNSET = object()`
sentinel. Expanded `test_gate_dry_run_context.py` from 20 to 55 tests
covering 14 representative scenarios (idle, source mutation, forbidden
mutation, policy-forbidden, backend known/unknown, adoption, commit, push,
all-flags). Decision-equivalence invariants verified across all scenarios:
gate count=15, names/order preserved, hard blocks denied, authorization/
enforcement always false, audit evidence shape lists, no redaction applied.
Memoization verified: _detect_task_contract 15→1 call, git evidence ≤3
calls per invocation. Freshness confirmed across separate invocations.
No persistent cache, no global cache, no module-level mutable state.
No tests deleted/skipped/xfailed. No assertions weakened. No production
behavior changed beyond sentinel fix. Doc at docs/PHASE_88_GATE_DRY_RUN_
DECISION_EQUIVALENCE_AND_PERFORMANCE_MATRIX.md. Next: 88Z.

### 88Y.3 — Gate Dry-Run Shared Evidence Prototype (2026-06-27)

Performance optimization. Implemented `GateDryRunContext` lazy-memoized
dataclass in new `src/pcae/core/gate_dry_run_context.py`. Modified
`build_gate_dry_run()` and `_evaluate_gate()` to use shared context instead
of 15× repeated `_detect_task_contract` calls and redundant git subprocess
calls. Eliminated second `build_risk_register` cascade by deriving risk
evidence from `project_state` snapshot. Added 20 tests for decision
equivalence, memoization, freshness, and no-persistence. Single
`build_gate_dry_run()` call: 20.86s→9.16s (-56%). Gate/phase87 tests:
~990s→558s (-44%). Full suite: 34:16→25:18 (9,010 tests, -26%).
No gate decisions changed. No persistent cache. No test deletion/skip/xfail.

### 88Y.2 — Gate Dry-Run Performance Profiling and Optimization Design (2026-06-27)

Design-only phase. Profiled `build_gate_dry_run()`: 1,087 git subprocess
calls per invocation due to cascading nested build function dependencies
(artifact_index called 32×, memory_snapshot 16×, governance_timeline 8×,
decision_log 4×, risk_register 2×). Gate evaluation is <0.03s out of 17s.
Designed `GateDryRunContext` with lazy-memoized properties to eliminate
redundant computation. Expected: 88-94% runtime reduction (17s→1-2s per
call). No production code changes. Design doc at docs/PHASE_88_GATE_DRY_RUN_
PERFORMANCE_PROFILING_AND_OPTIMIZATION_DESIGN.md. Next: 88Y.3 prototype.

### 88Y.1 — CLI Subprocess Runtime Reduction (2026-06-27)

Test optimization. Converted test_phase87_integration.py from subprocess
CLI calls to direct function calls. Individual improvements up to 16%.
Full suite: 8,956 passed / 34:16. build_gate_dry_run() identified as
dominant bottleneck. No production changes, no test deletion.

### 88X.1 — Idle-State Full Suite Baseline Repair (2026-06-27)

Baseline investigation. Confirmed 185 full-suite failures from 88X were
not reproducible in idle state. Root cause: active task contract during
88X run interfered with preflight tests using `subprocess.run` against
`REPO_ROOT`. Full suite: 8,800 passed / 0 failed in 33:00. No source or
test changes. Documented fixture pattern for future preflight hardening.

### 88X — Advisory Mode Prototype (2026-06-27)

Implements the first advisory mode prototype. Adds `pcae advisory check`,
`pcae advisory explain`, and `pcae advisory status` — non-authorizing commands
that wrap broker + shell gate infrastructure and produce would-* advisory
decisions. New core mapper in `src/pcae/core/advisory.py` maps all 25 broker
decisions to 19 advisory decisions. CLI handlers in `src/pcae/commands/advisory.py`.
105 fast-green tests in `tests/test_advisory_mode.py`. All invariants preserved:
no command execution, shell interception, wrappers, backend invocation, or
authorization. 88V.1 secret redaction and hard-block preservation maintained.
Fast-green: 2,814 passed (up from 2,709).

### 88V.1 — Secret Redaction and Deny Mapping Repair (2026-06-27)

Enforcement-readiness repair phase. Fixes four gaps documented in 88U/88V:

- **GAP-1 VAR=val secret redaction**: Secret-like VAR=val command prefixes
  (OPENAI_API_KEY, TOKEN, PASSWORD, etc.) now detected as secret_access with
  full command redaction in broker output.
- **GAP-2 env/printenv secret exposure**: `env` and `printenv` removed from
  read-only programs; now classified as secret_access.
- **GAP-3 broker.requested_command redaction**: `broker.requested_command`
  now redacted when secret_access detected; serialized JSON output is safe.
- **GAP-4 deny mapping**: Shell-gate `deny` now maps to `blocked_by_shell_gate`
  (a hard block decision), closing enforcement boundary gap.

Source changes: `src/pcae/core/shell_gate.py` (added
`_is_secret_env_var_name`, `_SECRET_VAR_NAME_SUBSTRINGS`, env/printenv handler,
fixed path stripping for VAR=val), `src/pcae/core/permission_broker.py`
(requested_command redaction, deny mapping fix). 43 new fast-green tests
(2,709 total). No enforcement, shell interception, or backend invocation.

- Broker + Shell Gate Enforcement Boundary Design (Phase 88V): design-only phase. Defines what must be true before PCAE can move from read-only command classification/aggregation into any enforcement, command gating, shell wrapping, or execution-control prototype. Explicitly documents that four 88U findings block enforcement until repaired: (GAP-1) VAR=val secret command not redacted — env_var_prefix pattern does not check value against known-secret var names, value leaks into audit trail; (GAP-2) env|grep and printenv secret exposure not detected — both classified as read_only_inspection despite potential secret output; (GAP-3) broker.requested_command retains raw secret-access command text — only shell_gate_evidence.command_text redacted, not the outer broker field; (GAP-4) "deny" dormant in _SG_HARD_BLOCK_TO_BROKER — not in BPE_HARD_BLOCK_DECISIONS, so hard_block_present=False if "deny" were ever produced. Delivers `docs/PHASE_88_BROKER_SHELL_GATE_ENFORCEMENT_BOUNDARY_DESIGN.md` (version 0.1, draft_documented, implementation_status=not_started, recommended_next_phase=88V.1_secret_redaction_and_deny_mapping_repair). 30 required sections: (1) Purpose — 4 explicit obligations (PCAE read-only; enforcement not next step; each stage needs own design; hard blocks permanent); (2) Scope — design artifacts only, nothing implemented; (3) Non-goals — 19 must-not items verbatim; (4) Current state from 88T/88U — what exists (classifier, broker, CLI, 8652 tests) and what does not exist (no interception, no blocking, no wrappers, no persistent state); (5) Enforcement terminology — 10 defined terms (classification, aggregation, gate, enforcement, advisory gate, blocking gate, execution gate, hard block, redaction, enforcement blocker); (6) Read-only classifier boundary — Stage 0 current state, all performed flags unconditionally False, what allow_preflight_only means at Stage 0; (7) Advisory gate boundary — Stage 2 future, no blocking, agent may disregard; (8) Blocking gate boundary — Stage 5 future, 10 minimum requirements; (9) Execution gate boundary — Stage 6+ future, all blocking gate requirements plus 9 additional; (10) What PCAE may do now — 10 authorized actions; (11) What PCAE must not do yet — 14 prohibited actions; (12) Enforcement preconditions — 9 preconditions (redaction completeness, secret detection completeness, mapping completeness, audit completeness, contradiction detection, performed-flag invariant, operator disable path, rollback procedure, separate design approval); (13) 88U findings as enforcement blockers — GAP-1 through GAP-4 with root cause, enforcement risk, and required repair for each; (14) Secret redaction requirements — scope (all broker-visible fields), sentinel, hash behavior, timing, test requirements; (15) requested_command redaction requirements; (16) env/printenv/VAR=val handling requirements — 3 patterns (VAR=val prefix, env|grep, printenv <VAR>) with known-secret pattern set; (17) deny mapping consistency requirements — 4 rules (explicit mapping, hard-block consistency, fail-closed, no dormant mappings); (18) Human approval limits — 7 permanent limits; (19) Accepted risk limits — 7 permanent limits; (20) Hard-block non-override rules — 7 rules; (21) Audit requirements — 26-field minimum audit record with source and notes; (22) Performed-flag invariants — 14 flags unconditionally False including under enforcement paths; (23) Contradiction detection requirements — 5 rules; (24) CLI output safety requirements — 10 rules; (25) Persistent state/cache restrictions — 6 rules; (26) Shell wrapper restrictions — 9 rules including no-default, reversible, no-capture, no-modify; (27) Disable/rollback strategy — 4 requirements (operator-visible disable, rollback procedure, no silent failure, no enforcement as default); (28) Test requirements before enforcement — 9 test sets with blockers marked (redaction coverage, VAR=val detection, deny mapping, requested_command, performed-flag, contradiction, hard-block non-override, disable path, fast-green preservation); (29) Enforcement staging roadmap — Stage 0 (current, read-only), Stage 1 (readiness repair — required before any enforcement), Stage 2 (advisory-only gate), Stage 3 (explicit dry-run blocking simulation), Stage 4 (opt-in command wrapper prototype), Stage 5 (limited blocking enforcement), Stage 6 (broader enforcement), plus forbidden shortcuts (no stage skipping, no temporary enforcement without disable path, no default enforcement, no combined repair+enforcement, no hard-block override); (30) Recommended next phase — 88V.1 with 4 specific source changes required (VAR=val in shell_gate.py, env|grep/printenv in shell_gate.py, broker.requested_command in permission_broker.py, deny mapping in permission_broker.py) and full deliverables list. No source changes. No test changes. No shell interception. No enforcement. No backend invocation. No shell wrappers. No persistent state. Fast-green: 2,666 passed / ~26s (unchanged from 88U baseline). Recommends 88V.1 — Secret Redaction and Deny Mapping Repair.

- Broker + Shell Gate Integration Test Expansion and Edge-Case Review (Phase 88U): pressure-tests the 88T broker + shell gate integration prototype with 120 new fast-green tests across 13 test classes in new file `tests/test_broker_shell_gate_edge_cases.py`. No source changes (no narrow defects found requiring fixes). Verified: compound commands (&&/||/; with spaces through broker — most restrictive segment wins by `_CATEGORY_SEVERITY`; semicolon-without-spaces documented limitation: shlex yields `status;` as single token → classified as unknown); pipe+tee writes (tee README.md → blocked_by_scope; tee src/ → blocked_by_task_contract no-task or requires_more_evidence with task; tee -a flag correctly skipped by `_find_tee_write_target`); environment mutation variants (export/unset/source/./VAR=val all → requires_human_review; VAR=val with secret value NOT redacted — documented false negative); network access (curl/wget/ssh/scp/ping all → requires_human_review; not hard blocks); package install (pip/pip -r/python -m pip/npm all → requires_human_review); unknown command conservative blocking (unknown-tool/customtool/./myscript.sh/bash all → blocked_by_shell_gate hard block — bash is a documented false positive); secret access edge cases (cat ~/.ssh/config, ~/.aws/credentials, ~/.kube/config, ~/.netrc, ~/.ssh/id_ed25519, ~/.gnupg/private-keys-v1.d all → secret_access + redacted + hash=null; security find-generic-password → secret_access; cat src/ → not redacted; broker.requested_command retains raw value even for secrets — documented redaction scope limitation); expensive pytest classification without subprocess (python -m pytest -n auto/-n 4/pytest --numprocesses all → expensive_test_execution_detected=True; plain pytest/python -m pytest tests → False); CLI JSON envelope stability (schema_version, generated_at, repository_root, broker dict, decision in BPE_DECISIONS, authorization_granted=False, execution_authorized=False, all 14 performed flags=False, shell_gate_evidence present/absent based on --requested-command, secret command redacted in sg_evidence.command_text); idle vs active task boundary across all command types (read-only: allow regardless; cp no-task: blocked_by_task_contract; cp with-task: requires_more_evidence; pytest no-task: blocked_by_task_contract via 1d; pytest with-task: allow; env_mutation action no-task: blocked_by_task_contract via p5; raw/force push: always hard block); non-hard-block authorization invariant (parametrized: authorization_granted and execution_authorized always False including after human_review allow_preflight_only); hard-block mapping consistency (_SG_HARD_BLOCK_TO_BROKER all values in BPE_DECISIONS, all keys in SGP_DECISIONS, blocked_by_scope+blocked_by_task_contract confirmed in BPE_HARD_BLOCK_DECISIONS); documented false negatives/positives: (FN-1) VAR=val env prefix not redacted — env_var_prefix pattern does not check value for secrets; (FN-2) env | grep KEY → read_only_inspection; (FN-3) printenv KEY → read_only_inspection; (FP-1) bash script.sh → blocked_by_shell_gate (conservative); (FP-2) git reset HEAD~1 → blocked_by_shell_gate (only --hard/--mixed handled); (FP-3) semicolon-without-spaces; (SI-1) "deny" in _SG_HARD_BLOCK_TO_BROKER but not in BPE_HARD_BLOCK_DECISIONS (dormant inconsistency); (RSL-1) broker.requested_command not separately redacted for secret commands. Fast-green: 2,666 passed / 25.74s (was 2,546; +120). Quick tier: 7,915 passed / 2:33 (was 7,807; +108 non-slow). Full suite: 8,652 passed / 28:57 (was 8,532; +120). Adds `docs/PHASE_88_BROKER_SHELL_GATE_INTEGRATION_EDGE_CASE_REVIEW.md`. Recommends 88V — Broker + Shell Gate Enforcement Boundary Design.

- Broker + Shell Gate Integration Prototype (Phase 88T): implements first prototype integration between permission broker and shell gate classifier. Changes to `src/pcae/core/permission_broker.py`: (1) Updated `_SG_HARD_BLOCK_TO_BROKER` — `blocked_by_policy_forbidden_file` now maps to `blocked_by_scope` (was `blocked_by_shell_gate`; consistent with scope preflight audit trail) and `blocked_by_missing_task` now maps to `blocked_by_task_contract` (was unmapped; now a hard block at priority 1); (2) Added constants `_SG_ALLOW_DECISIONS`, `_SG_HARD_BLOCK_DECISIONS_SET`, `_SG_PERFORMED_FORBIDDEN_KEYS`, `_SG_SCHEMA_VERSION`; (3) Added `_check_sg_contradiction(sg_evidence, requested_action, human_approval_present, accepted_risk_present) → list[str]` — 13 contradiction conditions per 88S §15: schema version mismatch, any of 14 performed/authorization flags True in sg_evidence or detected_flags, hard_block_present=True with allow decision, force_push_detected with non-force-push decision, raw_git_push_detected with allow decision, unknown category with allow decision, mutating action with allow_read_only decision, secret not redacted when secret_access_detected, human approval alongside SG hard block, accepted risk alongside SG hard block; (4) Updated `_broker_decide` to 9-priority chain — added priority 1d (SG requires_active_task + no task → blocked_by_task_contract hard block; fires before existing hard block map check) and priority 2 (contradiction detection via passed contradiction_details → blocked_by_conflicting_evidence; fires after priority 1 which means priority 1 hard blocks still win but contradictions are flagged in audit); added `contradiction_details` parameter; (5) Updated `build_permission_broker` — sg_evidence now includes schema_version ("0.1"), command_text_redacted flag, hard_block_present computed from _SG_HARD_BLOCK_DECISIONS_SET, secret_access_detected mirrored from detected_flags; command text replaced with `<redacted_secret_access_command>` when secret_access_detected=True before any storage; calls `_check_sg_contradiction` before `_broker_decide` and passes contradiction_details; 13 new audit fields added to broker dict (shell_gate_schema_version, shell_gate_command_category, shell_gate_command_text_hash [SHA-256 of command; null if redacted], shell_gate_command_text_redacted, shell_gate_decision, shell_gate_reason_codes, shell_gate_hard_block_present, conflicting_evidence_detected, conflicting_evidence_details, hard_block_sources, human_review_sources, accepted_risk_noted, broker_mapping_reason); evidence_source label for shell gate now includes category name; SHA-256 via stdlib hashlib (no new dependency). New test file `tests/test_broker_shell_gate_integration.py` — 162 fast-green integration tests across 12 test classes: hard-block propagation (14), non-hard-block handling (8), read-only commands (7), contradiction detection (18 including direct _broker_decide call to demonstrate priority 2 firing when no SG hard block), performed-flag invariant (56 parametrized: 14 flags × 4 decision paths — allow, hard block, human review, contradiction), secret redaction (7), active-task boundary (7), audit fields (15), decision mapping (9), sg_evidence fields (10), envelope invariants (8), CLI smoke (3, slow/integration). All 14 performed/authorization flags unconditionally False across all decision paths. No shell interception. No execution authorization. No backend invocation. No prompts/capture/intake/adoption. No shell wrappers. No persistent state. Existing broker tests: 150 passed unchanged. Shell-gate regression: 611 passed. Fast-green: 2,546 passed / 23.39s. Quick tier: 7,807 passed / 2:36. Full suite: 8,532 passed / 1:00:48. Adds `docs/PHASE_88_BROKER_SHELL_GATE_INTEGRATION_PROTOTYPE.md`. Recommends 88U — Broker + Shell Gate Integration Test Expansion and Edge-Case Review.

- Broker + Shell Gate Integration Design (Phase 88S): design-only phase producing `docs/PHASE_88_BROKER_SHELL_GATE_INTEGRATION_DESIGN.md` (version 0.1, status draft_documented, implementation_status not_started). Defines how the permission broker prototype should consume and interpret shell-gate evidence in a future 88T integration prototype. Covers: (1) Evidence fields — 21 shell-gate fields the broker must consume, fields to reject (performed/authorization flags if true), and command text redaction policy (SHA-256 hash when secret_access_detected; no raw text in audit records); (2) Full decision mapping — all 26 SGP_DECISIONS → 24 BPE_DECISIONS with priority column and hard-block flag; key changes from 88R: `blocked_by_missing_task` → `blocked_by_task_contract` promoted to priority 1 hard block (was falling through to missing evidence), `blocked_by_policy_forbidden_file` → `blocked_by_scope` for audit consistency with scope preflight, `requires_active_task` + no task → `blocked_by_task_contract` hard block; (3) Category mapping — all 24 SGP_CATEGORIES with broker implications and hard-block column; (4) 12-level integrated decision priority chain for 88T `_broker_decide`: SG hard blocks (1a force push, 1b raw git push, 1c SG hard block map, 1d requires_active_task+no_task) → malformed/contradictory evidence → evidence failures → test run lock → no active task → scope denial → missing evidence → human review → allow_preflight_only; (5) Hard-block propagation rules for force push, raw git push, destructive filesystem, policy-forbidden file, test run lock, and unknown — all unconditional, no human approval or accepted risk override; (6) Non-hard-block handling: `requires_human_review` satisfied by human_review_present; `requires_preflight` → missing evidence + scope check; `requires_active_task` when task present → no block; `requires_more_evidence` → missing evidence; all SG allow decisions → allow_preflight_only maximum; (7) Human approval limits — satisfies human-review gate only; never overrides hard blocks; does not grant execution authorization; (8) Accepted risk limits — recorded in evidence; never overrides hard blocks; never satisfies human review gate; (9) Missing SG evidence — requires_more_evidence (never allow); (10) Contradiction detection — 7 specific contradictions all → `blocked_by_conflicting_evidence` hard block; (11) Performed-flag invariant — all 14 flags unconditionally false, invariant survives hard blocks, human approval, accepted risk; (12) Audit model — 11 new fields for 88T: shell_gate_schema_version, shell_gate_command_category, shell_gate_command_text_hash, shell_gate_command_text_redacted, shell_gate_decision, shell_gate_reason_codes, shell_gate_hard_block_present, conflicting_evidence_detected, conflicting_evidence_details, hard_block_sources, human_review_sources, accepted_risk_noted, broker_mapping_reason; (13) Security requirements — schema version validation (block if missing or wrong), malformed evidence type checking (unknown category or allow decision + hard_block=True → contradiction), conservative handling (block when uncertain), no trust amplification (SG allow ≠ execution authorization); (14) Minimum 102-test suite specification for 88T (hard-block propagation 8+, non-hard-block 6+, read-only 3+, malformed evidence 5+, performed-flag invariant 56 parametrized, secret redaction 2+, contradiction 4+, active-task boundary 4+); (15) Recommended implementation sequence: 88T prototype → 88U validation → 88V schema hardening; (16) 20 safety invariants. No source files modified. No tests added or changed. Fast-green: 2,384 passed / 22.20s. Recommends 88T — Broker + Shell Gate Integration Prototype.

- Broker Test Task-Contract Decoupling (Phase 88R.1): repairs `tests/test_permission_broker.py` so 19 tests that require active-task-present broker behavior use an isolated `tmp_task_root` fixture instead of live `REPO_ROOT`. Root cause: after `pcae task finish` returned the repo to idle, `_detect_task_contract(REPO_ROOT)` returned `None`; the broker correctly applied its priority-4 rule (`blocked_by_task_contract` for all mutating actions without an active task) before reaching the downstream decision branches those tests expected (`allow_preflight_only`, `requires_more_evidence`, `requires_human_review`, `blocked_by_scope`). The broker behavior was correct; the test design coupled test outcomes to live repo state. Fix: (1) added `tmp_task_root` pytest fixture in `tests/test_permission_broker.py` — uses pytest `tmp_path`, creates `tasks/active/test-active-task.md` with minimal allowed-files content (`src/**`, `tests/**`, `docs/**`), fully isolated per-test; (2) added optional `root: Path = REPO_ROOT` parameter to `_pb()` helper and updated `build_permission_broker` call; (3) updated exactly 19 test methods (Group A: 5 tests in `TestAllowPreflightOnly` — all mutating-action allow paths; Group B: 7 tests in `TestRequiresMoreEvidence`; Group C: 6 tests in `TestRequiresHumanReview`; Group D: 1 test in `TestScopePreflight` — `test_policy_forbidden_file_blocked_by_scope`). No-active-task blocking tests (`TestBlockedByTaskContract`, `test_hard_block_takes_priority_over_no_task`, `test_health_failure_priority_over_task_contract`) preserved unchanged — still use explicit empty-root dirs. Tests that are inherently task-agnostic (read actions, shell-gate hard blocks, evidence failures via `health_passed=False`) also preserved unchanged. No source files modified (`src/pcae/core/permission_broker.py` untouched). Broker decision priority unchanged. No tests deleted. No tests skipped. No xfail added. Fixture kept module-local (not in `conftest.py` — only used in this file). `README.md` correctly denied via global `_SPF_POLICY_FORBIDDEN_FILES` policy without needing it in the fixture's forbidden list. Targeted broker tests: 150 passed. Shell-gate regression: 449 passed, 0 failed. Fast-green: 2,384 passed / 23s. Quick tier: 7,648 passed / 2:21. Full suite: 8,370 passed / 29:24, 0 failures. - Permission Broker Prototype (Phase 88R): implements `pcae permission-broker evaluate` — a read-only decision aggregator that consumes PCAE governance evidence and returns a conservative broker decision envelope. Never executes commands, invokes backends, sends prompts, writes storage, or grants real execution authorization. All 14 performed/authorization flags (`authorization_granted`, `execution_authorized`, `command_executed`, `repo_mutation_performed`, `backend_invocation_performed`, `prompt_sent`, `capture_performed`, `intake_performed`, `adoption_performed`, `commit_performed`, `push_performed`, `raw_git_push_performed`, `force_push_performed`, `storage_written`) unconditionally false. Evidence collection: task contract detection (internal, `_detect_task_contract`), shell gate classification (internal, `_classify_command` + `_decide` — no execution), scope preflight (internal, `build_scope_preflight` — when action+files provided), doctor test-run (subprocess via `_call_doctor_test_run` — only when expensive pytest detected), plus explicit evidence flags: `--health-passed`, `--check-passed`, `--doctor-passed`, `--push-check-passed`, `--tests-present`, `--tests-passed`, `--human-review-present`, `--human-approval-present`, `--accepted-risk-present`. Decision priority chain (8 levels): (1) shell gate hard blocks — force push > raw git push > raw git commit > history rewrite > destructive filesystem > policy forbidden > other; (2) explicit evidence failures — health > check > doctor > tests > push check; (3) test run lock (when expensive test execution detected); (4) no active task for mutating actions; (5) scope preflight denial; (6) missing evidence → `requires_more_evidence`; (7) human review gate → `requires_human_review`; (8) all clear → `allow_preflight_only`. 24 broker decision values in `BPE_DECISIONS`. Mutating actions require active task: `source_mutation`, `test_mutation`, `docs_mutation`, `filesystem_write`, `environment_mutation`, `adoption`, `commit`, `push`, `rollback`, `storage_write`, `backend_invocation`. Missing evidence for mutating actions: health and governance check required; push also requires push check. Human review gate: `push`, `commit`, `adoption`, `rollback`, `storage_write`, `backend_invocation` require `--human-review-present`. Scope preflight integration: `blocked_by_scope`, `deny_preflight`, `blocked_by_lifecycle_state`, `blocked_by_missing_task_contract`, `blocked_by_must_never_repeat_control`, `blocked_by_risk` all map to broker blocks. Policy-forbidden files (README.md, docs/REAL_CAPTURED_TASKS.md, docs/LINKEDIN_ARTICLE_DRAFT.md) remain hard blocks via scope preflight. New modules: `src/pcae/core/permission_broker.py` (`build_permission_broker`, `BPE_DECISIONS`, `BPE_HARD_BLOCK_DECISIONS`, `BPE_MUTATING_ACTIONS`, `_broker_decide`), `src/pcae/commands/permission_broker.py` (`run_permission_broker_evaluate`). CLI registration in `src/pcae/cli.py`: `permission-broker` top-level command with `evaluate` subcommand (follows shell-gate pattern). Adds `tests/test_permission_broker.py` — 150 tests across 14 test classes: `TestEnvelopeInvariants` (6), `TestBrokerKeyInvariants` (14), `TestPerformedFlagInvariants` (56 parametrized — 14 flags × 4 scenarios), `TestSafetyNotes` (6), `TestAllowPreflightOnly` (8), `TestRequiresMoreEvidence` (7), `TestRequiresHumanReview` (7), `TestBlockedByTaskContract` (3), `TestShellGateHardBlocks` (8), `TestEvidenceFailures` (8), `TestScopePreflight` (4), `TestBPEConstants` (5), `TestEvidenceProvided` (6), `TestPermissionBrokerCLI` (10 subprocess). All fast tests added to fast-green tier. Fast-green: 2,384 passed / 22.67s (was 2,234; +150 broker tests). Full suite: TBD. Adds `docs/PHASE_88_PERMISSION_BROKER_PROTOTYPE.md`. Recommends 88S — Permission Broker Expansion.

- Shell Gate Test Matrix and False-Positive Review (Phase 88Q): hardens the Phase 88P shell gate classifier by adding compound command parsing, pipe/tee write detection, backend/secret/environment classification, and a comprehensive command-category test matrix. Classifier changes to `src/pcae/core/shell_gate.py`: (1) compound command parsing — `&&`, `||`, `;` operators split token list into segments; most-restrictive category (by `_CATEGORY_SEVERITY` ordering) wins; reason code `compound_command_detected` prepended; (2) pipe/tee write detection — `cmd | tee <path>` detects tee target, classifies write category (`policy_forbidden_file_mutation` / `source_mutation` / `test_mutation` / `docs_mutation` / `filesystem_write`); pure pipe chains use most-restrictive segment; (3) `_BACKEND_PROGRAMS` frozenset — `claude`, `claude-deepseek`, `codex`, `openai`, `anthropic`, `gemini`, `vertex` → `backend_invocation` (previously `unknown`); (4) `_SECRET_ACCESS_PROGRAMS` frozenset — `security`, `pass`, `gpg`, `op`, `vault`, etc. → `secret_access`; (5) `_SECRET_FILE_PREFIXES` — `cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa`, `cat ~/.aws/credentials`, `cat ~/.kube/config`, etc. → `secret_access` (previously `read_only_inspection` FALSE NEGATIVE); (6) environment mutation: `export VAR=val`/`unset VAR` → `environment_mutation`, `source file`/`. file` → `environment_mutation`, `VAR=val cmd` env-var prefix → `environment_mutation`; (7) filesystem permission changes: `chmod`, `chown`, `chgrp`, `chattr`, `ln` → `filesystem_write` (previously `unknown`); (8) `python -m pip install` → `package_install` (previously `unknown`). Internal refactor: `_classify_command` renamed to `_classify_single`; new `_classify_command` wrapper handles compound/pipe routing; new helpers: `_empty_flags`, `_split_on_operators`, `_find_tee_write_target`, `_most_restrictive_classification`, `_is_secret_file_access`. False negatives fixed: `echo x | tee README.md` → `policy_forbidden_file_mutation`; `cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa` → `secret_access`; `git status && rm -rf /` → `destructive_filesystem`; `pcae health && git push` → `raw_git_push`. All 155 existing `tests/test_shell_gate.py` tests preserved unchanged. New `tests/test_shell_gate_matrix.py`: 287 tests across 24 test classes (category matrix, idle/active, compound, pipe/tee, redirection, backend/secret/environment, performed-flag invariant, boundary, false-positive review, false-negative review, helper unit tests). `tests/conftest.py` updated: `test_shell_gate_matrix` added to `FAST_GREEN_MODULES`. Creates `docs/PHASE_88_SHELL_GATE_TEST_MATRIX.md`. Classifier-only boundary preserved: no execution, no shell interception, no shell wrappers, no backend invocation, no permission broker, all performed flags unconditionally false. Fast-green: 2,234 passed / 22.66s (was 1,947). Quick tier: 7,508 passed / 2:08 (was 7,221). Full suite: 8,220 passed / 0:27:24, 0 failures (was 7,933). Recommends 88R — Permission Broker Prototype.

- Shell Gate Prototype (Phase 88P): implements the first shell gate classifier as a read-only command analysis command `pcae shell-gate check --command "<cmd>" [--json]`. Classifies proposed shell commands into 23 categories (88O taxonomy) and returns one of 26 decision values with a structured JSON envelope. Never executes the command text. New source: `src/pcae/core/shell_gate.py` (classifier + `build_shell_gate`), `src/pcae/commands/shell_gate.py` (CLI runner), CLI registration in `src/pcae/cli.py`. Classification: read-only programs (ls, pwd, cat, grep, find, sed -n, awk) → `allow_read_only`; git read-only subcommands → `allow_read_only`; `git push` → `blocked_by_raw_git_push`; `git push --force/-f/--force-with-lease` → `blocked_by_force_push`; `git commit` → `blocked_by_raw_git_commit`; `git rebase/reset --hard/cherry-pick` → `blocked_by_history_rewrite`; `rm -rf`/`git clean -fd` → `blocked_by_destructive_filesystem`; output redirection `>` to README.md/REAL_CAPTURED_TASKS.md/LINKEDIN_ARTICLE_DRAFT.md → `blocked_by_policy_forbidden_file`; redirection to `src/**` → `source_mutation`; `tests/**` → `test_mutation`; `docs/**` → `docs_mutation`; `pip/brew/npm/cargo install` → `requires_human_review`; `curl/wget/ssh/aws/gh` → `requires_human_review`; `python -m pytest -n auto` → `allow_test_execution` (with test-run preflight check) or `blocked_by_test_run_lock`; `pcae commit/push` → `allow_governed`; all other pcae subcommands → `allow_governed`; unrecognized program → `blocked_by_unknown_command`. All performed flags unconditionally false (`authorization_granted`, `execution_authorized`, `command_executed`, `repo_mutation_performed`, `backend_invocation_performed`, `prompt_sent`, `capture_performed`, `intake_performed`, `adoption_performed`, `raw_git_push_performed`, `force_push_performed`, `storage_written`). Policy-forbidden files checked via `_SGP_POLICY_FORBIDDEN_FILES` tuple (identical to `_SPF_POLICY_FORBIDDEN_FILES`). Expensive pytest (`-n` flag) calls `pcae doctor test-run --json` read-only to check `clear_to_run`. Adds `tests/test_shell_gate.py` with 155 fast unit tests (all fast-green tier) across 11 test classes: envelope invariants (10), performed flags always false (80 parametrized), read-only commands (12), raw git commit blocked (4), raw git push blocked (4), force push blocked (5), history rewrite blocked (3), destructive filesystem blocked (4), file write/redirection (5), policy-forbidden file (5), test execution (6), package/network review (5), unknown command (4), pcae governed (4), safety notes (5). Fast-green: 1,947 passed / 22.60s (was 1,792 — 155 new tests added). Quick tier: 7,221 passed / 2:11 (was 7,066). Full suite: 7,933 passed, 0 failed / 28:45. Known limitations: compound commands (`&&`/`;`) only examine first token; shell variable expansion not evaluated; `tee` pipe chain writes not detected; categories backend_invocation/prompt_send/capture/intake/adoption/environment_mutation/secret_access have no program lists yet (conservative: classified as unknown → blocked). Recommends 88Q — Shell Gate Test Matrix and False-Positive Review.
- Scope Matching Shared Utility Reconciliation (Phase 88O.1): eliminates the scope file-pattern matching divergence between `gate_dry_run.py::_evaluate_scope` (which used inline logic: `fnmatch.fnmatch(rf, pat) or rf == pat or rf.startswith(pat.rstrip("*"))`) and `scope_preflight.py::_match_file` (the canonical function already used by `mutation_preflight` and `backend_preflight`). The divergence was: `gate_dry_run` lacked the `if stripped and ...` empty-string guard around its `startswith` check, meaning pattern `"*"` → `stripped=""` → `rf.startswith("")` = always True without the fnmatch guard; `_match_file` would skip that branch since `fnmatch.fnmatch(rf, "*")` already returns True. Fix: in `gate_dry_run.py::_evaluate_scope`, extend the existing late import (`_SPF_POLICY_FORBIDDEN_FILES`) to also import `_match_file`, remove the local `import fnmatch`, and replace the two inline `any()` matching loops with `_match_file(rf, forbidden_patterns)` / `_match_file(rf, list(allowed_patterns))`. No new shared module created; late-import approach maintains the existing circular-import workaround. No other source files changed. Adds `tests/test_scope_matching_consistency.py` with 42 tests: 12 `_match_file` unit tests (exact/glob double-star/single-star/prefix/wildcard/empty), 8 `_SPF_POLICY_FORBIDDEN_FILES` constant tests, 12 Python-level cross-caller consistency tests (all four callers agree on forbidden/allowed classification with mock task contract), 4 no-active-task non-authorising tests (blocked_by_missing/unknown/None/scope_not_evaluated), 5 subprocess CLI consistency tests (scope preflight + gate dry-run + mutation preflight + backend preflight all block README.md; cross-CLI agreement test). Documents prefix-fallback behavior: `_match_file("README.md.bak", ["README.md"])` = True because `startswith("README.md")` — current documented behavior, not changed. Adds `docs/PHASE_88_SCOPE_MATCHING_SHARED_UTILITY_RECONCILIATION.md`. Pre-edit targeted baseline: 168 passed. Post-edit: all 168 tests pass unchanged (22 scope_gate, 63 scope_preflight_review, 47 backend_preflight_review, 36 mutation_preflight_review). Fast-green: 1,792 passed / 31.40s. Quick tier: 7,066 passed / 2:37. Full suite: green (see PROJECT_STATUS.md). Recommends 88P — Shell Gate Prototype.
- Shell Gate Design Reconciliation (Phase 88O): reconciles the Phase 87 shell gate architecture with the concrete Phase 88/88N preflight layer, permission broker reconciliation, fast-green validation architecture, and policy-forbidden consistency work. Delivers `docs/PHASE_88_SHELL_GATE_RECONCILIATION.md` — design-only artifact (version 0.1, draft_documented, implementation_status=not_started). Defines: shell gate role (future mediation layer that observes proposed commands, classifies risk, requires preflight evidence, blocks raw push/force push/policy-forbidden mutations, never executes itself); shell gate non-role (not an executor, not the permission broker, not a replacement for preflights/task-contracts/human-review/pcae health/check/doctor); relationship to permission broker (broker decides policy in principle, gate controls shell execution in practice — both needed, neither replaces the other); relationship to all five explicit preflights (scope/backend/mutation/commit/push outputs are evidence inputs, not authorization); relationship to task contracts (gate enforces but does not define; policy-forbidden files are hard blocks independent of task contract content); no-active-task conservative policy (read-only inspection allowed, all mutating/invocation/test categories require active task or are blocked); command classification taxonomy (23 categories: read_only_inspection, test_execution, pcae_governed_lifecycle, pcae_governed_commit, pcae_governed_push, raw_git_commit, raw_git_push, force_push, git_history_rewrite, destructive_filesystem, filesystem_write, source_mutation, test_mutation, docs_mutation, policy_forbidden_file_mutation, backend_invocation, prompt_send, output_capture, intake_adoption, package_install, network_access, secret_access, environment_mutation, unknown); decision model (26 values: allow_read_only through unknown; unknown always treated as deny); raw git commit policy (blocked when pcae governed path available); raw git push / force push (unconditional hard blocks, no human override at gate level); destructive filesystem policy (default deny, narrow authorization path); shell redirection classified as filesystem_write; package install always requires_human_review; backend/network/API commands require preflight + active task + human review; prompt/capture/intake/adoption gated by full governance chain; test execution policy with test-run preflight requirement (clear_to_run=true before full-suite); tier-aware validation (targeted + fast-green for low/medium risk; quick for pre-push confidence; full for shared governance source changes); fast-green integration (gate must not downgrade or collapse tier model); policy-forbidden file hard blocks independent of task contract; human approval and accepted-risk limits (evidence not bypass; force push blocked even with human approval; accepted risk ≠ mitigation); audit and evidence model (decision_id, reason_codes, command_class, risk_class, evidence_artifacts, 8 audit event types); known gate_dry_run.py scope matching divergence from scope_preflight.py::_match_file (inline fallbacks rf==pat and rf.startswith vs pure fnmatch; documented as risk for future shell gate; corrective phase 88O.1 recommended); future roadmap 88O.1 (scope match shared utility) → 88P (shell gate prototype) → 88Q (test matrix) → 88R (broker prototype) → 88S (broker+gate integration); 17 safety invariants. Design only: no source changes, no test changes, no shell gate implementation, no permission broker implementation, no backend invocation, no shell interception, no storage. Fast-green: 1,792 passed, 21.19s. Quick tier: deferred (design-only phase). Full suite: deferred (prior baseline 88N.6: 7,736 passed / 0 failed). Recommends 88O.1 — Scope Matching Shared Utility Reconciliation.
- Preflight Policy-Forbidden Consistency Repair (Phase 88N.6): restores full-suite green baseline by propagating `_SPF_POLICY_FORBIDDEN_FILES` into the three scope evaluation functions that previously consumed only `task_contract["forbidden_files"]` directly. Root cause: `_evaluate_scope_for_mutation` (`mutation_preflight.py`), `_evaluate_scope_for_files` (`backend_preflight.py`), and `_evaluate_scope` (`gate_dry_run.py`) all skipped the policy-forbidden file merge that `scope_preflight.py`'s `_evaluate_preflight` had already received in Phase 88N.3. The 88N.4 "zero failures" baseline was task-state-dependent: the 88N.4 task contract explicitly listed `README.md`, `docs/REAL_CAPTURED_TASKS.md`, and `docs/LINKEDIN_ARTICLE_DRAFT.md` in its forbidden-files section, making the tests pass accidentally. The 88N.5 task did not list them, exposing the gap. 10 tests in `test_mutation_preflight_review.py`, `test_backend_preflight_review.py`, `test_backend_preflight.py`, `test_mutation_preflight.py`, and `test_scope_gate.py` failed (all expecting `blocked_by_scope` or `out_of_scope` for policy-forbidden files; receiving `requires_human_review` or `unknown`). Fix: three-line merge pattern (identical to 88N.3) applied to each of the three evaluation functions. `gate_dry_run.py` uses a late import inside `_evaluate_scope` to avoid the existing circular import with `scope_preflight.py`. No test file changes. No assertions weakened. No tests deleted. No skip/xfail. Fast-green architecture from 88N.5 preserved: 1,792 tests, 21.72s. Targeted preflight tests: 181 passed, 0 failed (was 10 failed before repair). Quick tier: 7,029 passed in 2:22. Full suite green. Documents repair in `docs/PHASE_88_PREFLIGHT_POLICY_FORBIDDEN_CONSISTENCY_REPAIR.md`. Recommends 88O — Shell Gate Design Reconciliation.
- Fast Green Validation Architecture (Phase 88N.5): defines a practical 1–2 minute normal development validation gate. Adds 17 structural self-verification tests in `tests/test_88n5_fast_green_validation.py` (marker declaration, conftest wiring, collection bounds, inclusion/exclusion policy, docs artifact). Documents tier model (targeted / fast-green / quick / full), selection criteria, policy for when each tier is appropriate, and remaining limitations in `docs/PHASE_88_FAST_GREEN_VALIDATION_ARCHITECTURE.md`. Quick tier: 7,029 passed in ~2:29. Fast-green invocation: `python -m pytest -m "fast_green" -n auto -ra --durations=50`. Recommends 88O — Shell Gate Design Reconciliation.
- Full Suite Bottleneck Elimination (Phase 88N.4): profiles and eliminates the dominant full-suite runtime bottleneck (28:13 / 1,693s on M5 Pro). Root cause: 115 tests across `test_project_state.py`, `test_risk_register.py`, `test_decision_log.py`, and `test_governance_timeline.py` each called `_run_<command>_json()` independently per test, spawning a fresh Python subprocess per assertion (7–30s each). These files cover PCAE governance commands (project-state, risk-register, decision-log, governance-timeline) whose output never changes between test calls in the same run. Fix: replaced per-test subprocess calls with `@pytest.fixture(scope="module")` fixtures that run each command once per xdist worker and cache the result for all field-checking tests in the module. Determinism tests (e.g., `test_risk_register_risks_are_deterministic`) share two module-scoped runs via `_<name>_data2()` fixture instead of 2 subprocess calls per test (previously 6 subprocess calls total for 3 determinism tests, now 2 per worker). No-mutation behavioral tests (`test_*_no_repository_files_created`, `test_*_no_cache_files_created`) retain own subprocess calls since they require pre/post state comparison. Cross-command smoke tests (`test_*_still_works`) retain own calls since they test distinct commands. Adds `docs/PHASE_88_FULL_SUITE_BOTTLENECK_ELIMINATION.md`. Quick tier: 7,012 passed in 2:21 (was 5:27 — 2.3× speedup). Full suite: 7,719 passed in 23:20 (was 28:13 — 5-minute / 17% improvement). No tests deleted, no assertions weakened, no tests marked slow/xfail for speed. Remaining bottlenecks documented: 23 test_agent.py 44c capability-discovery tests (~4.5s each, capsys-bound), 8 no-mutation behavioral tests (must keep own subprocess), 15 cross-command smoke tests (intentional redundancy). Recommends 88O — Shell Gate Design Reconciliation.
- Scope Preflight Review Full-Suite Baseline Repair (Phase 88N.3): repairs 2 pre-existing failures in `tests/test_scope_preflight_review.py` confirmed present on the 88N.1 and 88N.2 baselines. Root cause: `docs/LINKEDIN_ARTICLE_DRAFT.md` was absent from both the 88N.1 and 88N.2 task contracts' forbidden file lists; the scope preflight is purely task-contract-driven, so the file was classified as unknown rather than forbidden — producing `requires_more_evidence` instead of `blocked_by_scope`, causing `test_forbidden_exact_match_linkedin` and `test_multi_file_two_allowed_one_forbidden` to fail. Fix: added `_SPF_POLICY_FORBIDDEN_FILES` constant to `src/pcae/core/scope_preflight.py` listing three PCAE governance documents always forbidden regardless of task contract (`README.md`, `docs/REAL_CAPTURED_TASKS.md`, `docs/LINKEDIN_ARTICLE_DRAFT.md`); merged via deduplication into `forbidden_patterns` at evaluation time in `_evaluate_preflight`. No test changes required — tests were already correctly asserting intended PCAE policy; the implementation was the divergence. Adds `docs/PHASE_88_SCOPE_PREFLIGHT_BASELINE_REPAIR.md`. Targeted: 63 passed. Related scope/preflight tests: 133 passed. Quick tier: 7,012 passed in 4:35. Full suite: 7,719 passed, 0 failures (prior baseline 88N.2: 7,717 passed, 2 failures). Baseline restored. Recommends 88O — Shell Gate Design Reconciliation.
- Full Suite Runtime Optimization and Test-Run Lock (Phase 88N.2): adds `pcae doctor test-run [--json]` — a read-only preflight that detects active expensive pytest (xdist) processes via `ps aux` pattern matching, preventing overlapping full-suite runs. Returns `clear_to_run=true/false` with `active_pytest_process_count`, `active_pytest_processes` list, and `policy` description. Detection: matches lines containing `python`+`pytest`+`-n\s*(auto|\d+)` (xdist parallel runs); ignores `ps aux`/`grep` lines and non-xdist sequential runs. Conservative: false positives acceptable; false negatives more dangerous; `ps` failure reports clear (cannot detect). Does not kill processes, does not start tests, does not write files. Adds 14 tests in `tests/test_doctor_test_run.py`: no-process detected, xdist found, -n4 found, ps-self filtered, collect-only ignored, multiple runs detected, shell-process-with-pytest-in-eval filtered (88N.2 regression: real false positive fixed — shell wrapper with `eval 'python -m pytest -n auto'` was being detected; fix: check COMMAND field starts with python, not /bin/sh|bash|zsh), clear/busy JSON, clear/busy text, no-mutate, no-backend-invocation, stale-ps-error-handled. Profiling finding: `test_project_state.py` (21 tests × ~8.4s sequential = ~176s) and `test_risk_register.py` are the top subprocess hotspots in the quick tier — both already marked slow. Quick tier: 6,998 tests, ~4 minutes with `-n auto` (18+ minutes without). Full suite: 7,705 tests. Documents tier policy: targeted / quick / governance / integration / full; full suite must be preceded by `pcae doctor test-run`. Source changed: `src/pcae/commands/task.py` (new `_detect_active_pytest_processes`, `run_doctor_test_run`), `src/pcae/cli.py` (import + `pcae doctor test-run` subcommand). Adds `docs/PHASE_88_FULL_SUITE_RUNTIME_OPTIMIZATION.md`. Targeted test result: 13 passed. Quick tier: 6,998 passed. Full suite: 7,717 passed, 2 pre-existing failures in test_scope_preflight_review.py (confirmed pre-existing on 88N.1 baseline; not regressions from 88N.2). Recommends 88N.3 — Scope Preflight Review Full-Suite Baseline Repair. 88O (Shell Gate Design Reconciliation) deferred until full-suite baseline is green.
- Task Finish Tracked-File Robustness (Phase 88N.1): fixes `pcae task finish --staged-file-aware --commit` so it succeeds when the active task contract file in `tasks/active/` was never tracked by git. Root cause: `run_task_finish` built `paths_to_stage` unconditionally starting with the old active path; after `finish_active_task` moved the file to `tasks/done/`, `git add -- tasks/active/...md` failed with "pathspec did not match any files" because git had no tracked record of that path. Fix: call `git ls-files --error-unmatch` on the active path before the move; include the old active path in `paths_to_stage` only when `returncode == 0` (tracked). Untracked case: `paths_to_stage` starts empty; `result.updated_files` and `result.completed_task.destination_path` provide the new done path, `tasks/DONE.md`, and session file — which are staged cleanly. Tracked case: behavior identical to before. Adds 8 regression tests to `tests/test_staged_file_aware_task_finish.py`: `test_untracked_task_sfa_finish_succeeds`, `test_untracked_task_sfa_finish_moves_to_done`, `test_untracked_task_sfa_finish_updates_done_md`, `test_untracked_task_sfa_finish_creates_commit`, `test_untracked_task_sfa_finish_no_staged_remainder`, `test_untracked_task_sfa_finish_no_pathspec_error`, `test_tracked_task_sfa_finish_still_works`, `test_untracked_task_finish_no_duplicate_done_entry`. Helper `_create_untracked_active_task` reproduces the 88M failure precondition. Adds `docs/PHASE_88_TASK_FINISH_TRACKED_FILE_ROBUSTNESS.md` documenting the 88M failure sequence, root cause, corrected behavior, and test coverage. Targeted task-finish tests: 50 passed. Quick tier: 6,998 passed. Full suite: deferred (source change is narrow; targeted tests cover the fix; prior clean baseline 7,640 from 88L.1; full-suite optimization is explicitly scheduled as 88N.2). Recommends 88N.2 — Full Suite Runtime Optimization and Test-Run Lock.

Integration sections for: approval (explicit scope, allowed files, source artifact, authorized≠performed, expire by explicit decision), denial (preserved, not silently reopened, appears in forbidden-action answers), deferral (requires reason and target, not approval, carried forward), rejection (requires reason, remains rejected unless explicitly reopened, visible in must-never-repeat), human override (requires authority and reason, must not erase original state, auditable), accepted risk (requires risk level and rationale, not mitigation, feeds risk register), permission (runtime decisions, do not auto-authorize lifecycle, allowed/blocked/escalated), must-never-repeat (captures unsafe patterns/violations/lessons, permanent unless superseded, surfaces in snapshot queries). 10 query targets: what_was_approved, what_was_denied, what_was_deferred, what_was_rejected, what_was_overridden, what_risk_was_accepted, what_permission_decisions_were_made, what_requires_human_review, what_can_be_safely_done_next, what_must_never_be_repeated — each with required decision types, artifact index/timeline/memory dependencies, expected answer shape, required provenance, safety caveats. 12 decision update rules. - Roadmap Reconciliation and Phase 85 Plan (Phase 84L): adds `docs/ROADMAP_RECONCILIATION_PHASE_85_PLAN.md`. Formally reconciles original Phase 84 persistent memory/project intelligence roadmap (84A–84F: persistent lifecycle memory, artifact index, governance event timeline, decision log integration, risk register, project state snapshot) with actual Phase 84 multi-agent governance design stream (84A–84K.3: 10 governance design artifacts, governance summary, health baselines, handoff refresh). Original roadmap deferred because 83A–83L lifecycle exposed prerequisite: stable lifecycle objects and governance semantics before persistent memory. Phase 84 created the concepts Phase 85 will build on. Proposed Phase 85 sequence: 85A Persistent Lifecycle Memory Model (inputs: lifecycle state machine, deferred tracker, health baseline), 85B Artifact Index (inputs: governance summary, all design artifacts), 85C Governance Event Timeline (inputs: changelog, project status, commit history), 85D Decision Log Integration (inputs: adoption candidate schema, deferred tracker, approval artifacts), 85E Risk Register (inputs: invocation guard, storage policy, deferred tracker), 85F Project State Snapshot (inputs: 85A–85E outputs, answers original Phase 84 questions). Each phase defined with purpose, inputs, expected output, implementation status=not_started, test expectations, safety boundaries. Phase 85 acceptance boundaries: memory does not authorize execution, indexing does not authorize adoption, decision log does not authorize commit/push, risk tracking does not auto-resolve, snapshot distinguishes observed from authorized. Test strategy: design-only phases may skip tests, first implementation phase must add tests, default `python -m pytest -n auto`, 3 serial exceptions retained. Implementation gates: no source without explicit phase, no test skipping, no backend without guard, no adoption without lifecycle. Deferred items carried forward: DF-1–DF-4, HY-1 (closed_no_action), IMPL-1, IMPL-2, TEST-1, HSR-1 (validator stale for doc streams). Handoff-state-refresh validator note: structural signals documented and non-blocking. Bootstrap note: modern test command documented. Recommends 85A as next phase. No Phase 85 task contract created. roadmap_reconciliation_name=phase_84_to_85_reconciliation, roadmap_reconciliation_version=0.1. No backend invocation, no implementation, no tests added, no source/test/README changes.

- Second Real Captured Task Selection (Phase 81A): adds `docs/SECOND_REAL_CAPTURED_TASK_SELECTION.md`. Selects a documentation-only task (lifecycle command family snippet) for the second governed backend-created output adoption lifecycle. No source code changes, no tests, no backend invocation.
- Lifecycle Final Summary (Phase 80F): adds `pcae lifecycle backend-output-adoption summary [--json]`. Aggregates lifecycle state, gate model (16 gates, 3 approval, 3 execution), next-step recommendation, artifact summary, command capabilities, safety flags, and blockers in one read-only report. Confirms `non_dry_run_runner_command=false` and all execution/approval/push flags false. Completes the 80A-80F lifecycle orchestration stream. 15 new tests.
- Lifecycle Gate Approval (Phase 80E): adds `pcae lifecycle backend-output-adoption approve-gate --gate <gate> --approved-by <name> --reason <reason> [--dry-run] [--json]`. Records human approval for a lifecycle gate without executing it. Requires explicit gate, approver, and reason. Blocks unknown gates, missing approver/reason, and illegal lifecycle states. Reports `approval_not_required` for non-approval gates. Always sets `execution_authorized=false` and all execution/push/backend flags to false. Dry-run previews approval without recording. 15 new tests.
- Lifecycle Gate Runner Dry-Run (Phase 80D): adds `pcae lifecycle backend-output-adoption run-gate --gate <gate> --dry-run [--json]`. Evaluates whether a named lifecycle gate would be runnable from the current state without executing it. `--dry-run` is required; calling without it blocks. 16 gate definitions cover the full adoption lifecycle. Reports gate kind, target state, required artifacts/approvals/preconditions, blockers, and planned action summary. Purely read-only: no gate execution, no approval, no backend invocation, no file mutation. 17 new tests.
- Lifecycle Advisory Batch (Phases 80A-80C): adds lifecycle state machine design (`docs/LIFECYCLE_STATE_MACHINE.md`), `pcae lifecycle backend-output-adoption status [--json]` (read-only lifecycle status), and `pcae lifecycle backend-output-adoption next [--json]` (read-only next-step recommendation). State model covers 17 states from idle through closed with artifact-based detection. Commands are purely advisory: they do not mutate state, invoke backends, run gates, or approve anything. 24 new tests.
- Governance Reliability Hardening (Phases 79D-79F): adds `pcae.hook_bypass` module for formal hook-bypass policy classification (9 tests), `pcae.artifact_metadata` module for artifact metadata consistency validation with strict/advisory modes (12 tests), and improved task-memory reconciliation coverage (9 tests). Hook bypass is forbidden by default; only bounded, documented exceptions with exact commit/file scope are allowed. Artifact metadata requires full SHA256; short prefixes are insufficient. Task memory repair never deletes files or modifies source code. 30 new tests total.
- Staged-File-Aware Push (Phase 79C): adds `--staged-file-aware` flag to `pcae push`. Pushes approved commits while preserving unrelated pre-existing staged files. Blocks if protected staged files appear in unpushed commit contents. Blocks force push. Verifies protected staged file blob hashes unchanged after push. Supports `--dry-run --json`. 10 new tests with local bare remotes.
- Staged-File-Aware Task Finish (Phase 79B): adds `--staged-file-aware` flag to `pcae task finish --commit`. When active, commits only task-finish paths using pathspec commit, preserving unrelated pre-existing staged files in the index. Verifies protected staged file blob hashes unchanged after commit. Skips the pre-existing changes blocker that normally blocks `--commit`. Reports `protected_staged_files_preserved`, `protected_staged_file_hashes_before/after` in JSON. Never pushes, invokes backend, or executes runner. 9 new tests.
- Staged-File-Aware Implementation Commit Mode (Phase 79A): adds `pcae commit implementation --message <msg> --path <path> [--path <path> ...] [--dry-run] [--json]`. Commits only explicitly requested paths while preserving unrelated pre-existing staged files in the index. Blocks if requested paths overlap with pre-existing staged files. Verifies protected staged file blob hashes are unchanged after commit. Supports dry-run. Never pushes, invokes backend, or executes runner. 10 new tests.
- Lifecycle Regression Suite (Phase 78E): adds `tests/test_lifecycle_regression.py` with 23 regression tests covering adoption execution gates, commit approval/execution safety, push approval/execution safety, final verification gates, tooling push decision gates, hook-bypass reconciliation, and parametrized backend/runner non-invocation checks across all lifecycle commands. No source code changes.

- Real Execution Disabled Proof Logic Fix (Phase 74W.3): fixes inverted proof logic in `pcae phase real-execution-disabled-proof`. The `authorized` check defaulted to `True` in `art.get("authorized", True)`, causing false-positive FAIL violations when artifacts lacked the `authorized` field. Changed to `art.get("authorized") is not True`, correctly treating missing `authorized` as safe. Proof now reports `proof_status=passed`, `real_execution_disabled=true` with zero violations in the safe state. No authorization enabled. 6 new tests.
- Session Bootstrap Agent Lock Rehydration (Phase 74W.2): `pcae session bootstrap --agent-id <id>` now automatically rehydrates the backend lock artifact (`.pcae/agent-locks/latest.json`) when the agent_id is a recognized lockable backend (claude-local, claude-deepseek, claude-kimi, codex, manual, noop). Compact bootstrap supports `--sync-lock` flag for explicit lock rehydration. JSON output includes `lock_rehydrated`, `lock_backend_name`, `lock_conflict`, `lock_synced`, `recognized_backend`. All `execution_authorized=false`. No backend invocation. 5 new tests.
- Handoff Lock Synchronization (Phase 74W.1): adds `--sync-lock` to `pcae phase handoff --next-agent <id> --sync-lock` to synchronize handoff next-agent with agent lock identity. Validates backend is a recognized lockable identity (claude-local, claude-deepseek, claude-kimi, codex, manual, noop), writes/updates `.pcae/agent-locks/latest.json`. Reports `lock_sync_requested`, `lock_sync_performed`, `lock_backend_name`, `lock_sync_blockers` in JSON output. Unknown backends blocked. `execution_authorized=false`. 6 new tests.: adds `pcae phase claude-deepseek-prompt-capture-smoke --json --save --allow-real-invocation` and `pcae phase claude-deepseek-prompt-capture-show --json`. Default smoke skips real invocation. Real invocation requires explicit opt-in, sends harmless deterministic prompt (PCAE_CAPTURE_OK), captures stdout/stderr under .pcae/claude-deepseek-prompt-captures/, runs mutation guard. Reports task_package_sent=false, task_implementation_requested=false, apply_performed=false. Show command reads latest capture artifact. 7 new tests.
- Claude-DeepSeek Prompt Capture Dry Run (Phase 74V): adds `pcae phase claude-deepseek-prompt-capture --dry-run --json --save` evaluating prerequisites for harmless output-only prompt capture. Checks lock, contract, enablement, safety review, git status. Reports would_send_prompt_text, would_send_task_package=false, would_request_task_implementation=false. All execution flags remain false. No backend invoked. 5 new tests.
- Claude-DeepSeek Prompt Capture Contract (Phase 74U): adds `pcae phase claude-deepseek-prompt-capture-contract --json --save` defining the harmless output-only prompt capture contract. Includes deterministic test prompt (PCAE_CAPTURE_OK), 20 requirements, 15 forbidden cases. All execution flags remain false. No backend invoked. 4 new tests.

No queue/task mutation. 6 new tests.

- Execution Authorization Design Record (Phase 72R): adds a formal design record to `docs/ARCHITECTURE.md` defining what execution authorization means and what it must not mean. - Queue Preflight Positive Non-Execution Path (Phase 72Q): adds 6 tests proving the positive non-execution path through runner preflight. With a valid fixture queue and matching approval, preflight correctly reports all queue-related requirements met (queue non-empty, queue validation present, queue valid, queue approval present, queue approval matches, queue approval execution_authorized=false) while execution remains `execution_available=false`, `execution_authorized=false`, and `preflight_status=design_only`. Human output clearly states no execution. Tests cover cleared queue revert and fixture cleanup.
- Queue Approval Matching Harden (Phase 72P): adds `pcae phase queue approval-check` and `--json` for a focused readiness check of queue approval state. Checks queue presence, queue validity, approval presence, approval digest match against current queue, and `execution_authorized=false`. Returns exit code 0 only when all checks pass. Tests prove match, mismatch after queue change, empty queue refusal, and execution_authorized=false using fixture queues. 6 new tests.
- Safe Queue Fixture Lifecycle (Phase 72O): adds `pcae phase queue fixture-add`, `--count N`, `--json` and `pcae phase queue fixture-clear`, `--json` for creating and safely removing non-executable test fixture entries. Fixtures are explicitly marked `source_type=fixture`, `fixture=true`, `execution_authorized=false` with deterministic titles (QUEUE-FIXTURE-001, -002, -003). Default count is 1, max is 3. `fixture-clear` removes only fixture entries, preserving all non-fixture entries. Queue validation now reports `fixture_count` and recognizes fixtures as valid. Validation only flags `execution_authorized=true` as forbidden (not `false`). 8 new tests.
- Queue-to-Runner Preflight Bridge (Phase 72N): extends `pcae phase runner-execution-preflight` to include real queue validation and queue approval status. Adds 5 new requirements: queue validation present, queue valid, queue approval present, queue approval matches current queue, and queue approval execution_authorized=false. Preflight output now includes `queue_validation_status`, `queue_valid`, `queue_approval_present`, `queue_approval_matches_current_queue`, and `queue_approval_execution_authorized`. Empty queue, invalid queue, and approval mismatch are detected and reported as unmet requirements. Execution remains `execution_available=false` and `execution_authorized=false`. Total requirements increased from 17 to 22. 7 new tests.
- Queue Approval Artifact (Phase 72M): adds `pcae phase queue approve`, `--json`, `--message`, and `--dry-run` for approving the current phase queue snapshot for future runner consideration. Requires queue validation to pass and queue to be non-empty. Refuses empty or invalid queues. Approval records `approved=true`, `approved_at`, `queue_digest` (SHA-256), `queue_entry_count`, `approval_message`, `approver_source=local_cli`, and `execution_authorized=false`. `--dry-run` reports proposed approval without writing. `pcae phase queue approval-show` and `--json` display the persisted approval including current queue digest match detection. Persists to `.pcae/phase-queue-approvals/latest.json`. No queue mutation, no task creation, no execution. 10 new tests.
- Real Queue Item Validation (Phase 72L): adds `pcae phase queue validate` and `--json` for read-only validation of real phase queue entries. Validates queue readability, entry titles, supported source_type, source_prompt_path for captured_prompt entries, placeholder/dummy detection, duplicate title detection, invalid phase_id patterns, and forbidden execution-authorizing fields. Empty queue is valid but reports `queue_ready=false`. No queue mutation, no task creation, no execution. 15 new tests.
- Execution Authorization Negative Gate (Phase 72K): adds `pcae phase runner-execution-authorize`, `--json`, and `--dry-run` as an explicit negative gate that always refuses execution authorization. - Compact Historical Continuity Summary (Phase 72I): compact bootstrap now summarizes historical strategic continuity in a single line showing decision ID, activation phase, decision basis, and first sentence of the rationale, followed by a "Full details:" pointer. Previously the full multi-paragraph rationale and deferred/referenced blocks were printed even when the decision was historical. Current (non-historical) strategic decisions continue to show full details. 4 new tests.
- Runner Execution Preflight Design (Phase 72H): adds `pcae phase runner-execution-preflight` and `--json` for a design-only preflight specification. Requires a review artifact with `ready_for_approval` status. Approval explicitly records `execution_authorized=false`. - Runner Simulation Failure Cases (Phase 72E): extends `pcae phase runner-simulate` with `--scenario` for failure case simulation using the 72B policy matrix. Supports 5 scenarios: `dirty-tree` (hard stop), `active-task` (hard stop), `git-lock` (recoverable stop, suggests `pcae doctor git-lock`), `audit-warning` (advisory warning), and `queue-empty` (continue allowed). - Runner Simulation Trace Artifact (Phase 72D): adds `pcae phase runner-simulate`, `--json`, `--save`, and `--count N` for dry-run simulation traces.
