- Added Execution Result Persistence (Phase 41D): `pcae remote execute JOB_ID --invoke` now captures execution timing and writes a first-class result artifact to `.pcae/remote/results/<job_id>-result.json`; artifact fields include `command`, `duration_seconds`, `executed`, `exit_code`, `final_status`, `finished_at`, `job_id`, `selected_agent`, `started_at`, `stderr` (full, untruncated), and `stdout` (full, untruncated); `_REMOTE_RESULTS_DIR` added as the canonical result directory (`Path(".pcae") / "remote" / "results"`); `started_at` and `finished_at` are captured as UTC ISO timestamps bracketing the subprocess call; `duration_seconds` is rounded to three decimal places; the job record is updated with `result_path` (canonical path to the new artifact) and `executed_at` (same as `started_at`); `invoke_remote_job` return dict gains `started_at`, `finished_at`, and `duration_seconds`; human output for `pcae remote execute --invoke` gains "Started at:", "Finished at:", and "Duration:" lines; `build_remote_results` reads from `results/<job_id>-result.json` first, falling back to the legacy `executions/<job_id>_result.json` path for pre-41D artifacts, and maps `started_at`/`finished_at` to the `execution_started_at`/`execution_finished_at` keys in the results dict; `.pcae/.gitignore` already covers `results/` via the existing `remote/` entry; `_REMOTE_RESULTS_DIR` added to core; `_run_remote_execute_invoke` updated in commands; 6 new tests cover results-dir artifact existence, timing field presence and type, job record update (result_path, executed_at), full stdout preservation (no truncation in artifact), timing fields populated in results report, and timing visible in human execute output.

- Added Governed Execution Reporting (Phase 41C): `pcae remote results JOB_ID` and `pcae remote results JOB_ID --json` expose execution results for persisted Remote Autonomous Coding jobs; reads the persisted job from `.pcae/remote/jobs/<JOB_ID>.json` and any adjacent execution artifact from `.pcae/remote/executions/<JOB_ID>_result.json`; exits 1 with a clear "Unknown job" message for unknown job IDs; reports `result_available: false` with a clear human message when no execution artifact is present; when an artifact is present, reports `job_id`, `requested_agent`, `command_used`, `execution_started_at`, `execution_finished_at`, `duration_seconds`, `exit_code`, `stdout_summary` (first 500 chars), `stderr_summary` (first 200 chars), `output_path`, `final_status`, and `readiness_at_execution` (all optional fields default to null when not recorded); advisory is `"Execution reporting is read-only; no agents are executed."`; JSON output includes `result_available`, `job_id`, `requested_agent`, `execution_result` (null or full result dict), and `advisory`; strictly read-only — no job files mutated, no agent executed, no approval state changed; `REMOTE_RESULTS_ADVISORY` and `build_remote_results(root, job_id)` added to core; `run_remote_results()` added to commands; `run_remote_results` imported and `results` subcommand wired in CLI; 7 new tests cover unknown job failure, no-artifact human output, no-artifact JSON structure, post-invoke JSON structure with all required keys, post-invoke human output, failed-job final_status, and read-only guarantee.

- Corrected Kimi Adapter Contract (Phase 41B.4): added kimi-local to `_build_invoke_command` returning `["kimi", "-p", prompt]`, matching the actual installed CLI contract confirmed by manual test (`kimi -p "..."` → success; positional invocation → `error: too many arguments`); extended `_derive_command_preview` to render `kimi -p '<prompt>'` for kimi-local (alongside the existing claude-local branch); no session-continuation, `--yolo`, or `--auto` flags used; stdout captured as-is without normalization; `test_remote_invoke_kimi_blocked` renamed to `test_remote_invoke_kimi_succeeds` and updated to assert exit 0, `executed=True`, and `command[:2]==["kimi","-p"]`; four new Phase 41B.4 tests added: dry-run command preview asserts `-p` present and `--prompt`/`--yolo`/`--auto` absent; invoke asserts `command[0]="kimi"`, `command[1]="-p"`; two regression tests confirm Codex and Claude adapters are unchanged; Codex and Claude adapters are unchanged.

- Validated Claude Adapter Contract (Phase 41B.3): corrected claude-local invocation from invalid `claude --print PROMPT` to `claude -p PROMPT` matching the actual installed CLI contract confirmed by manual test (`claude -p "..."` → output received); `_build_invoke_command` for `claude-local` now returns `["claude", "-p", prompt]`; `_derive_command_preview` for `claude-local` now renders `claude -p '<prompt>'` via a dedicated branch (Codex and other CLI agents are unchanged); kimi-local remains blocked ("syntax not safely derivable"); two new tests: `test_remote_execute_dry_run_command_preview_claude_uses_dash_p` asserts `-p` present and `--print`/`--prompt` absent in command preview; `test_remote_invoke_claude_command_uses_dash_p` asserts command[0]="claude", command[1]="-p", `--print` not in command.

- Synchronized Roadmap Recommendation After Real Execution (Phase 41B.2): `PREDICTED_PHASES_OPTION_C` updated from the stale `"37D Multi-Agent Collaboration Readiness"` (already recorded in DONE.md) to `"41C Governed Execution Reporting"` — the correct next phase in the active execution track; added `_filter_predicted_phases(root, phases)` helper that removes predicted phases whose phase code (e.g. "41C") appears as `Phase 41C` in any DONE.md entry line, preventing future staleness; recommendation rationale updated from "Option C — Multi-Agent Collaboration" to "Remote Coding execution track"; hardcoded human-output label `"Predicted phases (Option C — Multi-Agent Collaboration):"` updated to `"Predicted phases (Remote Coding):"`; `PROJECT_STATUS.md` current phase updated from `"Phase 39A: Remote Autonomous Coding Foundation."` to `"Phase 41B.1: Codex Adapter Contract Correction."`; two test assertions updated to match new rationale and label text; `pcae roadmap next` now recommends `41C Governed Execution Reporting`; `pcae governance sync-check`, `pcae governance audit`, and `pcae health` all remain valid.

- Corrected Codex Adapter Contract (Phase 41B.1): replaced invalid `codex --quiet PROMPT` invocation (which produced `error: unexpected argument '--quiet' found`) with `codex exec --sandbox read-only PROMPT` matching the actual installed CLI contract; `_derive_command_preview` for `codex-local` now renders `codex exec --sandbox read-only '<prompt>'` instead of the generic `codex --prompt '...'` template; no other agent invocation behavior changed; two existing test assertions strengthened to verify `exec`/`sandbox`/`read-only` present and `--quiet` absent.

- Added First Real Controlled Agent Invocation (Phase 41B): `pcae remote execute JOB_ID --invoke` and `pcae remote execute JOB_ID --invoke --json` invoke the selected agent under PCAE governance; `--invoke` is mutually exclusive with `--dry-run` (both now handled by a single `execute` subcommand); missing both flags exits 1 with a clear message; calls the readiness gate and raises `ValueError` if the job is not ready; per-agent command building: `claude-local` → `["claude", "--print", prompt]`, `codex-local` → `["codex", "--quiet", prompt]`, all others (including `kimi-local`) → blocked with "syntax not safely derivable"; agent subprocess captured via `_run_agent_subprocess(command, timeout)` (300 s default, extracted for testability); `subprocess.TimeoutExpired` and `FileNotFoundError`/`OSError` surfaced as clear `ValueError`s; `job["status"]` updated to `"completed"` (exit 0) or `"failed"` (non-zero) and written back to the job file; execution artifact written to `.pcae/remote/executions/<job_id>_result.json`; no commit or push performed; JSON output has `executed`, `job_id`, `selected_agent`, `command`, `exit_code`, `stdout`, `stderr`, `output_path`, `final_status`, and `advisory "Agent execution completed under PCAE governance; no commit or push was performed."`; human output shows all fields with stdout/stderr summary; `REMOTE_INVOKE_ADVISORY`, `_REMOTE_EXECUTIONS_DIR`, `_build_invoke_command()`, `_run_agent_subprocess()`, and `invoke_remote_job()` added to core; `_run_remote_execute_dry_run()` and `_run_remote_execute_invoke()` split from `run_remote_execute()`; `invoke_remote_job` imported; `--invoke` flag added (mutually exclusive with `--dry-run`) to CLI; 14 new tests cover missing flags, unknown job, pending/denied job blocked, runtime not installed blocked, success JSON structure, status=completed on disk, status=failed on disk, artifact written, no commit/push, advisory text, human output, kimi blocked, and dry-run regression.

- Added First Controlled Agent Execution Preview (Phase 41A): `pcae remote execute JOB_ID --dry-run` and `pcae remote execute JOB_ID --dry-run --json` preview execution of a persisted job without invoking any agent; `--dry-run` is required — omitting it exits 1 with a clear message; exits 1 for unknown or malformed jobs; calls the readiness gate internally to evaluate the job before building the preview; output includes `job_id`, `selected_agent`, `execution_mode`, `readiness_status` (ready/blocked), `prompt_preview` (first 200 chars of `requested_task`), `command_preview` (derived from `executable_hint` when adapter is CLI, otherwise null), `required_checks`, `required_approvals`, `blockers`, `safety_notes`, and `dry_run_result` (would_execute/blocked); advisory is `"Execution preview only; no agent was invoked."`; JSON output has `execution_preview` and `advisory`; strictly read-only — no files modified; `REMOTE_EXECUTE_DRY_RUN_ADVISORY`, `_derive_command_preview()`, and `build_remote_execute_dry_run(root, job_id)` added to core; `run_remote_execute()` added to commands; `run_remote_execute` imported and `execute` subcommand wired in CLI; 12 new tests cover JSON structure, approved-job fields, denied-job blocked, pending-job blocked, missing-dry-run failure, unknown-job failure, human output, advisory text, read-only guarantee, prompt-preview truncation, command-preview for CLI agent, and safety notes.

- Added Remote Execution Readiness Gate (Phase 40H): `pcae remote ready JOB_ID` and `pcae remote ready JOB_ID --json` evaluate whether a persisted job is ready for execution; reads `.pcae/remote/jobs/<JOB_ID>.json`; exits 1 with a clear message for unknown or malformed jobs; runs 13 named checks — `job_schema_valid`, `status_ready`, `approval_state_approved`, `policy_compliance`, `agent_allowed`, `adapter_allowed`, `execution_mode_allowed`, `runtime_installed`, `non_interactive_supported`, `git_working_tree_clean`, `pcae_check_required`, `tests_required`, `required_approvals_listed`; failing hard checks produce blocker messages; advisory warnings surfaced for git/pcae_check/tests/approvals items; `ready` is True only when all blockers are empty; human output shows readiness status, job_id, agent, checks-passed count, blockers, warnings, and advisory; JSON output has `ready`, `job_id`, `requested_agent`, `checks`, `blockers`, `warnings`, and `advisory "Execution readiness is advisory; no agent is executed."`; strictly read-only — no job files are created, modified, or deleted; `read_git_changes` imported; `REMOTE_JOB_READINESS_ADVISORY` and `check_remote_job_readiness(root, job_id)` added to core; `run_remote_ready()` added to commands; `run_remote_ready` imported and `ready` subcommand wired in CLI; 12 new tests cover JSON structure, approved-job status checks pass, denied job not ready, pending job not ready, unknown job failure, malformed job failure, human output, advisory text, read-only guarantee, all expected check keys present, job_id in output, and schema-invalid job produces blocker.

- Added Remote Job Approval Mutation (Phase 40G): `pcae remote approve JOB_ID` and `pcae remote deny JOB_ID` (each with `--json`) mutate the `approval_state` of a persisted job; approve sets `approval_state` to `"approved"` and `status` to `"ready"` when `policy_compliance.compliant` is true, otherwise `"draft"`; deny sets `approval_state` to `"denied"` and `status` to `"blocked"`; both commands exit 1 with a clear message for unknown or malformed jobs; human output shows job_id, previous approval state, new approval state, status, and advisory; JSON output has `updated`, `job`, `previous_approval_state`, `new_approval_state`, and `advisory "Approval state updated; no agent execution has occurred."`; mutation is written back to disk with `json.dump(indent=2, sort_keys=True)`; no agents are executed, no prompts submitted; `REMOTE_JOB_APPROVAL_ADVISORY`, `_mutate_job_approval()`, `approve_remote_job()`, and `deny_remote_job()` added to core; `_run_remote_approval_mutation()`, `run_remote_approve()`, and `run_remote_deny()` added to commands; `run_remote_approve` and `run_remote_deny` imported and `approve`/`deny` subcommands wired in CLI; 12 new tests cover approve JSON, deny JSON, status-ready-when-compliant, status-blocked-on-deny, human output (approve and deny), unknown job failure (approve and deny), malformed job failure, file mutation on disk (approve and deny), and advisory text.

- Added Remote Job Inspection (Phase 40F): `pcae remote jobs show JOB_ID` and `pcae remote jobs show JOB_ID --json` display full details for a single persisted job; reads `.pcae/remote/jobs/<JOB_ID>.json`; exits 1 with a clear error when the job ID is unknown or the file is malformed (invalid JSON or non-dict content); human output shows all 11 schema fields (job_id, requested_agent, requested_task, execution_mode, status, approval_state, created_at, policy_compliance, required_checks, required_approvals, safety_notes) plus advisory text; JSON output has `job` (full job dict) and `advisory "Job inspection is read-only; no agents are executed."`; strictly read-only — no files are created, modified, or deleted; `REMOTE_JOB_INSPECT_ADVISORY` and `inspect_persisted_job(root, job_id)` added to core; `run_remote_jobs_show()` added to commands; `run_remote_jobs_show` imported and `show` subcommand (with positional `job_id` and `--json`) wired in CLI as a sibling of `list` under the `jobs` subparser; 10 new tests cover JSON output, human output, unknown job failure, malformed JSON failure, non-dict JSON failure, all 11 fields present, advisory text (JSON and human), read-only guarantee, and human output section headings.

- Added Remote Job Listing (Phase 40E): `pcae remote jobs list` and `pcae remote jobs list --json` display persisted jobs from `.pcae/remote/jobs/` sorted newest first; `jobs` is now a subparser group with a `list` subcommand (`required=False` so existing `pcae remote jobs` behavior is preserved); `load_persisted_jobs(root)` reads all `*.json` files in the jobs directory, sorts by filename in reverse order (newest first), skips malformed files with a warning, and handles a missing directory gracefully; human output shows job count, per-job id/agent/approval/created-at, and any warnings; JSON output has `job_count`, `jobs` (full job objects), `warnings`, and `advisory "Job listing is read-only; no agents are executed."`; no job files are created, modified, or deleted; `REMOTE_JOBS_LIST_ADVISORY` and `load_persisted_jobs()` added to core; `run_remote_jobs_list()` added to commands; `run_remote_jobs_list` imported and `list` subcommand wired in CLI; 15 new tests cover empty directory, no jobs dir, JSON structure, persisted jobs visible, newest-first sort, job fields present, human output, advisory text, malformed file warning (json error and non-dict), mixed valid+malformed, read-only, all three allowed agents, and job_count == len(jobs).

- Hardened Remote Job Identity (Phase 40D.1): job IDs now include microsecond precision (`job-YYYYMMDD-HHMMSS-FFFFFF`) preventing collisions between jobs created in the same second; `_generate_unique_job_id(jobs_dir)` helper loops until it finds a path that does not yet exist on disk, then returns both the job_id and its file path; `persist_remote_job()` now uses `_generate_unique_job_id()` before building the job dict and opens the file with `"x"` (exclusive-create) mode so overwrites are impossible at the OS level; `build_remote_create_persist_preview()` also updated to the microsecond format for preview/persist consistency; the persisted filename always equals `{job_id}.json`; seven new tests cover microsecond format, filename-matches-job_id, 5 rapid jobs all unique, first-job-not-overwritten-by-second, `_generate_unique_job_id` skips pre-existing files, and preview-mode microsecond format.

- Added Real Remote Job Persistence (Phase 40D): `pcae remote create --agent AGENT_ID --prompt TEXT --persist` and `--json` persist a remote job definition to `.pcae/remote/jobs/` without executing agents or submitting prompts; `--persist` is mutually exclusive with `--dry-run` and `--preview-persist` — the required mutually exclusive group now has three members; unknown agents exit 1 with a clear error; disallowed agents (known but not in policy's allowed_agents) exit 1 with a clear "not allowed" error and create no file; the persisted job file contains exactly the 11 schema fields (job_id, requested_agent, requested_task, execution_mode, approval_state, policy_compliance, status, created_at, required_checks, required_approvals, safety_notes) with status=draft, approval_state=pending, and three safety notes confirming no agent has been executed, no prompt has been submitted, and human approval is required before any execution; the jobs directory `.pcae/remote/jobs/` is created if absent; the file is written with `json.dump(indent=2, sort_keys=True)`; human output reports job created, job id, selected agent, persisted path, status, approval state, and advisory "Job persisted. No agent execution has occurred."; JSON output includes `persisted: true`, `job_path`, `job` (full job dict), and `advisory`; `remote/` added to `.pcae/.gitignore`; `REMOTE_PERSIST_ADVISORY`, `_REMOTE_PERSIST_SAFETY_NOTES`, and `persist_remote_job()` added to core; `_run_remote_create_persist()` and dispatch in `run_remote_create()` added to commands; `--persist` added to CLI mutually exclusive group.

- Added Remote Job Persistence Preview (Phase 40C): `pcae remote create --agent AGENT_ID --prompt TEXT --preview-persist` and `--json` preview what a remote job would look like when persisted, without writing any files or executing agents; `--preview-persist` is mutually exclusive with `--dry-run` — at least one must be present; unknown agents exit 1; output includes `job_file_path` (e.g. `.pcae/remote/jobs/job-YYYYMMDD-HHMMSS.json`), `output_directory` (`.pcae/remote/jobs/`), `job_preview` (same schema as dry-run but with `persist_preview: true` instead of `dry_run: true`, and job_id prefixed `job-`), `validation` result, and advisory; job preview includes all required schema fields plus `persist_preview: true`; three safety notes confirm no job file is written, no agent will be executed, and preview is for planning only; `REMOTE_PERSIST_PREVIEW_ADVISORY`, `_REMOTE_PERSIST_PREVIEW_SAFETY_NOTES`, `_REMOTE_JOBS_OUTPUT_DIR`, and `build_remote_create_persist_preview()` added to core; `_run_remote_create_persist_preview()` and dispatch in `run_remote_create()` added to commands; `--dry-run` changed from `required=True` to part of a required mutually exclusive group with `--preview-persist` in CLI; all operations are strictly read-only with no file creation, agent execution, prompt submission, or state mutation.

- Added Remote Job Creation Dry Run (Phase 40B): `pcae remote create --agent AGENT_ID --prompt TEXT --dry-run` and `--json` preview creation of a remote job without persisting or executing it; `--agent`, `--prompt`, and `--dry-run` are all required — missing `--dry-run` fails with a clear argparse error (exit code 2); unknown agents exit 1; output includes a job_preview with all 11 job schema fields (plus `dry_run: true`), validation result (valid, errors, warnings, blockers), and advisory; job_preview fields: job_id (preview-YYYYMMDD-HHMMSS), requested_agent, requested_task (prompt text), execution_mode, approval_state (pending), policy_compliance, status (draft), created_at, required_approvals, required_checks, safety_notes; job preview is run through `validate_remote_job()` — allowed agents validate clean, policy-excluded agents (e.g. pcae-native) produce blocked validation; three safety notes confirm no job is persisted, no agent will be executed, and preview is for planning only; `REMOTE_CREATE_DRY_RUN_ADVISORY`, `_REMOTE_CREATE_SAFETY_NOTES`, and `build_remote_create_dry_run()` added to core; `run_remote_create()` added to commands; `pcae remote create` subcommand with `--agent`, `--prompt`, `--dry-run`, `--json` wired in CLI; all operations are strictly read-only with no job persistence, agent execution, prompt submission, or state mutation.
- Added First Controlled Remote Autonomous Coding Dry Run (Phase 40A): `pcae remote dry-run --agent AGENT_ID --prompt TEXT` and `--json` generate an advisory execution preview without submitting prompts or executing agents; `--agent` and `--prompt` are required flags; unknown agents (not in policy or registry) exit code 1 with a clear error; agents in the registry but not in policy are allowed as "known" but produce a blocked result with an explicit "not in allowed_agents" blocker; output fields are selected_agent, prompt_preview (truncated at 200 chars), execution_mode, policy_compliance (agent_allowed, adapter_allowed, compliant, execution_mode_allowed), required_approvals (3 gates from policy), required_checks (3 checks from policy), adapter_capabilities (installed, non_interactive, remote, mcp, hooks, runtime_version), blockers (agent not in policy, not installed, adapter not allowed, non-interactive unsupported), dry_run_result (would_execute/blocked), and safety_notes; three safety notes confirm no agent was executed, prompt was not submitted, and this is a preview only; `REMOTE_DRY_RUN_ADVISORY`, `_REMOTE_DRY_RUN_SAFETY_NOTES`, `_REMOTE_DRY_RUN_PROMPT_PREVIEW_MAX`, and `build_remote_dry_run()` added to core; `run_remote_dry_run()` added to commands; `pcae remote dry-run` subcommand with `--agent`, `--prompt`, `--json` wired in CLI; all operations are strictly read-only with no agent execution, prompt submission, persistent job creation, file modification, commit, or push.
- Added Remote Execution Strategy (Phase 39H): `pcae remote strategy` and `pcae remote strategy --json` expose the advisory remote runtime selection strategy model; strategy fields include selection_strategy (default: human_selected), preferred_runtime (null), fallback_runtimes ([]), tie_break_rule (null), human_override_enabled (true), advisory_notes, and supported_strategies; four supported strategies declared (human_selected, capability_based, policy_based, registry_order) as `REMOTE_SELECTION_STRATEGIES`; four advisory notes state that human selection always takes precedence, PCAE must not silently choose when human selection is required, recommendations remain advisory, and runtime neutrality is preserved; human output displays all fields with (none) for null/empty values; `REMOTE_STRATEGY_ADVISORY`, `REMOTE_SELECTION_STRATEGIES`, `_REMOTE_STRATEGY_ADVISORY_NOTES`, and `build_remote_strategy()` added to core; `run_remote_strategy()` added to commands; `pcae remote strategy` subcommand wired in CLI; all operations are strictly read-only with no runtime switching, automatic selection, agent execution, or state mutation.
- Added Remote Execution Adapter Selection (Phase 39G): `pcae remote adapters` and `pcae remote adapters --json` recommend the best available runtime adapter for remote autonomous coding; eligible agents are evaluated from policy's allowed_agents list against runtime discovery, adapter model, and policy constraints; per-agent fields include adapter_type, eligible, eligibility_reason, hooks, mcp, missing_capabilities, non_interactive, policy_allowed, remote, runtime_installed, and runtime_version; eligibility requires adapter type in allowed_adapters, agent installed, and non-interactive confirmed; agents with unknown remote capability are eligible but noted in selection_notes; scoring prefers remote=yes (+2) over remote=unknown (+1) with deterministic tie-breaking by position in allowed_agents; recommended_remote_runtime is None with "No eligible remote runtime found." rationale when no agents qualify; kimi-local is represented conservatively with unknown remote capability surfaced in missing_capabilities and selection_notes; `REMOTE_ADAPTERS_ADVISORY`, `_score_remote_agent()`, and `build_remote_adapters()` added to core; `run_remote_adapters()` added to commands; `pcae remote adapters` subcommand wired in CLI; all operations are strictly read-only with no agent execution, prompt submission, job creation, or runtime state modification.
- Added Remote Execution Approval Workflow (Phase 39F): `pcae remote approvals` and `pcae remote approvals --json` expose the advisory approval workflow model; four approval states (pending, approved, denied, expired) exposed as `REMOTE_APPROVAL_STATES`; three approval gates (before_execution, before_commit, before_push) exposed as `REMOTE_APPROVAL_GATES` with per-gate required flag derived from policy (approval_required, require_human_approval_before_commit, require_human_approval_before_push) and human-readable description; pending approvals are collected from the job registry (jobs with approval_state=="pending"); the empty registry has no pending approvals; `build_remote_approvals(jobs=None)` accepts an optional jobs parameter for testing; `REMOTE_APPROVALS_ADVISORY`, `REMOTE_APPROVAL_STATES`, `REMOTE_APPROVAL_GATES`, `_REMOTE_APPROVAL_GATE_DESCRIPTIONS`, `_REMOTE_APPROVAL_GATE_POLICY_KEYS`, and `build_remote_approvals()` added to core; `run_remote_approvals()` added to commands; `pcae remote approvals` subcommand wired in CLI; no approval mutation, job creation, agent execution, or runtime state modification.
- Added Remote Job Validation (Phase 39E): `pcae remote validate` and `pcae remote validate --json` validate remote job definitions against policy; validation checks schema completeness (all 11 required fields present), status validity (must be a supported status), agent policy compliance (requested_agent in allowed_agents), execution mode compliance (execution_mode in allowed_execution_modes), policy_compliance.compliant flag, and required approvals/checks presence; warnings are raised for empty required_approvals (when policy requires approval), empty required_checks, and non-compliant policy_compliance; blockers are raised for disallowed agents or execution modes; errors are raised for missing schema fields or unsupported statuses; the empty job registry validates cleanly (valid=true, job_count=0, no errors/warnings/blockers); `validate_remote_job(job, policy)` and `build_remote_validate(jobs=None)` added to core (jobs parameter allows injecting test data without mutating the registry); `run_remote_validate()` added to commands; `pcae remote validate` subcommand wired in CLI; all operations are strictly read-only with no agent execution, prompt submission, job creation, lock mutation, or runtime state modification.
- Added Remote Job Definition Model (Phase 39D): `pcae remote jobs` and `pcae remote jobs --json` expose a read-only remote job registry; job schema fields (job_id, requested_agent, requested_task, execution_mode, approval_state, policy_compliance, status, created_at, required_checks, required_approvals, safety_notes) are exported as `REMOTE_JOB_SCHEMA_FIELDS`; seven supported statuses (draft, awaiting_approval, approved, blocked, ready, completed, failed) are exported as `REMOTE_JOB_SUPPORTED_STATUSES`; the registry is deterministically empty for this phase — no job creation, execution, or prompt submission; JSON output includes jobs, job_schema, supported_statuses, and advisory; human output reports job count, supported statuses, and advisory note "Remote jobs are advisory definitions; no agents are executed."; `REMOTE_JOBS_ADVISORY`, `REMOTE_JOB_SUPPORTED_STATUSES`, `REMOTE_JOB_SCHEMA_FIELDS`, and `build_remote_jobs()` added to core; `run_remote_jobs()` added to commands; `pcae remote jobs` subcommand wired in CLI; all operations are strictly read-only with no agent execution, prompt submission, job creation, lock mutation, or runtime state modification.
- Added Remote Execution Plan Model (Phase 39C): `pcae remote plan` and `pcae remote plan --json` generate an advisory read-only remote autonomous coding execution plan combining remote policy, runtime discovery, adapter model, and governance state; plan fields are requested_agent (default: codex-local, overridable via `--agent`), execution_mode (non_interactive), policy_compliance (agent_allowed, adapter_allowed, execution_mode_allowed, compliant), required_approvals (human approval required before execution/commit/push), required_checks (clean git working tree, pcae check must pass, tests must pass), safety_notes, blockers, readiness_status (ready/blocked), and governance_readiness (session_active, architecture_memory_present, active_task_present); blockers are generated when the requested agent is not in allowed_agents, not installed, adapter not in allowed_adapters, or installed but does not support the required execution mode; readiness_status is "ready" when no blockers exist and "blocked" otherwise; `REMOTE_PLAN_ADVISORY`, `REMOTE_PLAN_DEFAULT_AGENT`, `_REMOTE_PLAN_SAFETY_NOTES`, and `build_remote_plan()` added to core; `run_remote_plan()` added to commands; `pcae remote plan` subcommand with `--agent` and `--json` wired in CLI; plan is strictly read-only with no agent execution, prompt submission, lock mutation, job creation, or runtime state modification.
- Added Remote Autonomous Coding Execution Policy (Phase 39B): `pcae remote policy` and `pcae remote policy --json` report the advisory remote execution policy; policy fields are allowed_agents (claude-local, codex-local, kimi-local), allowed_adapters (cli), allowed_execution_modes (non_interactive), approval_required (true), require_clean_git (true), require_pcae_check (true), require_tests (true), require_human_approval_before_commit (true), require_human_approval_before_push (true), max_files_changed (null), max_runtime_minutes (null), and disallowed_operations (delete_branch, drop_table, force_push, rm_rf); human output lists all policy fields with boolean values shown as yes/no and null limits shown as (unlimited); JSON output includes all fields plus advisory; `REMOTE_POLICY_ADVISORY`, `_REMOTE_POLICY_DISALLOWED_OPERATIONS`, and `build_remote_policy()` added to core; `run_remote_policy()` added to commands; `pcae remote policy` subcommand wired in CLI; policy is conservative and approval-based; all operations are strictly read-only with no agent execution, prompt submission, lock mutation, or runtime state creation.
- Added Remote Autonomous Coding Foundation (Phase 39A): `pcae remote status` and `pcae remote status --json` report advisory readiness for remote autonomous coding based on runtime discovery, adapter model, governance state, and session context; readiness is one of not_ready (no agents installed), partially_ready (agents installed but non-interactive unconfirmed), or ready (at least one agent with confirmed non-interactive support); human output shows readiness state, available runtimes with non_interactive/mcp/hooks/remote per agent, supported adapters, missing capabilities (unknown capabilities for installed agents), governance readiness (session_active, architecture_memory_present, active_task_present), and safety notes; JSON output includes readiness_status, available_agents, supported_adapters, missing_capabilities, governance_readiness, safety_notes, and advisory "Remote Autonomous Coding readiness is advisory; no agents are executed."; `REMOTE_STATUS_ADVISORY`, `REMOTE_STATUS_READY`, `REMOTE_STATUS_PARTIALLY_READY`, `REMOTE_STATUS_NOT_READY`, `REMOTE_SAFETY_NOTES`, `build_remote_status()`, `_build_remote_governance_readiness()`, and `_check_architecture_memory_present()` added to core; `run_remote_status()` added to commands; `pcae remote status` subcommand wired in CLI; all operations are strictly read-only with no agent execution, prompt submission, lock mutation, or remote job creation.
- Added Modular Kimi Adapter Inspection (Phase 38E): `pcae agents adapter inspect kimi-local` and `pcae agents adapter inspect kimi-local --json` expose deep capability inspection for the Kimi CLI adapter using the same `CapabilityRecord` schema (name, status, source, notes) as Codex and Claude; capabilities are discovered conservatively from `kimi --help` output; `KIMI_ADAPTER_INSPECT_ADVISORY` ("Capabilities are discovered conservatively and may evolve with Kimi CLI versions.") is registered in `_ADAPTER_INSPECT_ADVISORY_BY_AGENT_TYPE` under the "kimi" agent type; unknown capabilities remain unknown without deterministic help-text evidence; JSON output includes agent_id, adapter_type, capabilities, execution_modes, executable_path, runtime_version, and advisory; all operations are strictly read-only with no Kimi execution, prompt submission, CLI task launching, or runtime state mutation.
- Added Modular Claude Adapter Inspection (Phase 38D): `pcae agents adapter inspect claude-local` and `pcae agents adapter inspect claude-local --json` expose deep capability inspection for the Claude CLI adapter using the same `CapabilityRecord` schema (name, status, source, notes) as Codex; capabilities are discovered conservatively from `claude --help` output; `CLAUDE_ADAPTER_INSPECT_ADVISORY` ("Capabilities are discovered conservatively and may evolve with Claude CLI versions.") is selected automatically for claude-type agents via `_ADAPTER_INSPECT_ADVISORY_BY_AGENT_TYPE`; the advisory in `run_agents_adapter_inspect` is now taken from `data["advisory"]` rather than a hardcoded constant, making it per-agent without further code changes; capability names, status values, and source are identical to Codex inspection; JSON output includes agent_id, adapter_type, capabilities, execution_modes, executable_path, runtime_version, and advisory; all operations are strictly read-only with no Claude execution, prompt submission, CLI task launching, or runtime state mutation.
- Added Modular Codex Adapter Inspection (Phase 38C): `pcae agents adapter inspect AGENT_ID` and `pcae agents adapter inspect AGENT_ID --json` expose deep capability inspection for any registered agent; for CLI agents probed by runtime discovery, each capability is represented as a `CapabilityRecord` with name, status (yes/unknown), source (help), and notes; the `_CAPABILITY_SPECS` tuple is the single extension point — adding a new Codex capability requires one new tuple entry, no other code changes; output separates "Discovered capabilities" (status=yes) from "Unknown capabilities" (status=unknown); JSON output includes agent_id, adapter_type, capabilities, execution_modes, executable_path, runtime_version, and advisory; execution_modes lists "interactive" and "non-interactive" when detected; for agents not in the runtime probe list (declared agents) all capabilities are unknown and execution_modes is empty; for probed agents not installed all capabilities are unknown; unknown agents exit 1 with "Agent not found"; advisory: "Capabilities are discovered conservatively and may evolve with Codex CLI versions."; `CapabilityRecord`, `CAP_SOURCE_HELP`, `CAP_SOURCE_MANUAL`, `ADAPTER_INSPECT_ADVISORY`, `_CAPABILITY_SPECS`, `_build_capability_records()`, `_unknown_capability_records()`, and `build_adapter_inspection()` added to core; all operations are strictly read-only with no Codex execution, prompt submission, CLI task launching, or runtime state mutation.
- Added Agent Adapter Model (Phase 38B): `pcae agents adapters` and `pcae agents adapters --json` list all eight governed agent adapter definitions combining static registry configuration with runtime discovery results; each adapter entry includes agent_id, adapter_type (cli/native/undeclared), lifecycle_status, runtime_installed (bool or null when not probed), runtime_version, supports_interactive, supports_non_interactive, supports_mcp, supports_hooks, supports_remote, and notes; `pcae agents adapter show AGENT_ID` and `pcae agents adapter show AGENT_ID --json` show the same fields for a single agent, with exit 1 and "Agent not found" for unknown IDs; adapter_summary reports total and per-type counts (cli=3, native=1, undeclared=4); codex-local, claude-local, and kimi-local (cli) are probed via `build_runtime_discovery()` and their runtime fields reflect discovered values; pcae-native (native) reports runtime_installed=true with version=null and all capability fields unknown; declared agents (deepseek, gemini, grok, perplexity) have runtime_installed=null and all capability fields unknown — capabilities are never assumed without evidence; advisory: "Adapter reporting is advisory; no agent runtime is modified."; `AgentAdapterEntry`, `ADAPTER_ADVISORY`, `build_agent_adapters()`, `get_agent_adapter()`, and `_build_adapter_entries()` added to core; all operations are strictly read-only with no agent execution, prompt submission, CLI launching, or runtime state mutation.
- Updated kimi-local agent status assumptions (Phase 38A.1): kimi-local promoted from `declared` to `available` in `MULTI_AGENT_REGISTRY` following confirmed CLI installation; `AGENT_CONFIG_REGISTRY` entry updated with `adapter_type=cli`, `executable_hint="kimi"`, `requires_manual_setup=False`, and accurate configuration notes; lifecycle summary now reports available=4, declared=4; `pcae agents runtime-discover` continues to detect kimi-local when kimi is on PATH, reporting installed, executable path, version, interactive, and non_interactive (detected from "non-interactively" in help output) as yes, with all remaining capabilities (stdin, prompt_file, structured_output, MCP, hooks, subagents, remote) as unknown pending deterministic evidence; no capabilities were promoted without keyword evidence; all operations remain strictly read-only.
- Added Agent Runtime Capability Discovery (Phase 38A): `pcae agents runtime-discover` and `pcae agents runtime-discover --json` inspect local CLI availability and capabilities for codex-local (codex), claude-local (claude), and kimi-local (kimi); each agent's capabilities include installed (bool), executable_path, version, interactive_supported, non_interactive_supported, stdin_prompt_supported, prompt_file_supported, structured_output_supported, mcp_supported, hooks_supported, subagents_supported, remote_supported, and known_limitations; detection is conservative — capabilities are reported as "yes" only when specific keywords are found in help output, and "unknown" otherwise (never "no"); codex probes include `codex exec --help`, `codex mcp --help`, and `codex mcp-server --help` for richer signal; version is extracted from `--version` output using a version-number regex; missing executables are handled gracefully with all capabilities "unknown"; `stdin=DEVNULL` and a 5-second timeout protect against interactive sessions or hangs; JSON output includes agents, discovery_summary (agents_checked, agents_installed, agents_not_installed), and advisory "Runtime discovery is advisory; the user remains authoritative."; `AgentRuntimeCapabilities`, `AgentRuntimeEntry`, `RuntimeDiscoveryResult`, `build_runtime_discovery()`, `_find_executable()`, `_run_probe()`, `_extract_version_string()`, `_cap_detect()`, `_discover_capabilities()`, and `_not_installed_capabilities()` added to core; all operations are strictly read-only.
- Added Multi-Agent Review and Validation (Phase 37H): `pcae collaboration reviews` and `pcae collaboration reviews --json` expose three advisory review workflow templates — implementation_review (implementer → reviewer → validator), documentation_review (author → reviewer → validator), and architecture_review (proposer → reviewer → validator); each step declares step_name, recommended_agent_role, purpose, required_lifecycle_status ("available" for all steps), and review_status (template default "pending"); four governed review statuses are exposed: pending, reviewed, validated, rejected; JSON output includes review_workflows, review_statuses, and advisory "Review workflows are advisory; no agents are executed or assigned automatically."; human-readable output shows review workflow count, workflow names, review statuses, ordered steps with role/min-status/review-status/purpose, and the advisory note; `ReviewWorkflowStep`, `ReviewWorkflow`, `REVIEW_WORKFLOWS`, `build_review_workflows()`, `REVIEW_ADVISORY`, `VALID_REVIEW_STATUSES`, and four `REVIEW_STATUS_*` constants added to core; all operations are strictly read-only.
- Added Multi-Agent Handoff Governance (Phase 37G): `pcae collaboration handoffs` and `pcae collaboration handoffs --json` expose a read-only derived handoff history by scanning provenance events for `agent_released` → `agent_acquired` pairs; each HandoffRecord includes source_agent, target_agent, timestamp, phase (active task ID when available), active_task, continuity_verified (True when agent_acquired immediately follows agent_released with no intervening events), architecture_memory_present (True when `.pcae/architecture-history.json` exists and has entries), summary (from the preceding phase_completed event), and warnings (malformed-record notices for missing agent IDs or unparseable timestamps); handoffs are returned most-recent first; a release without a following acquire is ignored; JSON output includes handoff_count, handoffs, and advisory "Handoff reporting is advisory; no handoff state is modified."; human output shows handoff count, ordered records, continuity status, and architecture memory status; `HandoffRecord`, `HandoffHistory`, `build_handoff_history()`, `HANDOFF_ADVISORY`, `_extract_handoff_records()`, `_has_architecture_memory()`, and `_is_valid_timestamp()` added to provenance core; all operations are strictly read-only.
- Added Collaboration Workflow Foundation (Phase 37F): `pcae collaboration workflows` and `pcae collaboration workflows --json` expose four deterministic advisory workflow templates — implementation (implementer → reviewer → validator), documentation (author → reviewer → validator), architecture (proposer → reviewer → validator), and handoff (outgoing_agent → incoming_agent → validator); each step declares step_name, recommended_agent_role, purpose, and required_lifecycle_status (minimum lifecycle state: declared/configured/available/active); the handoff workflow's outgoing_agent step requires status "active" (the agent must hold the session lock); all other steps require "available"; JSON output includes a workflows list and advisory "Collaboration workflows are advisory templates; no agents are executed or assigned automatically."; human-readable output shows workflow count, workflow names, ordered steps with role and minimum status, and purpose per step; `WorkflowStep`, `CollaborationWorkflow`, `COLLABORATION_WORKFLOWS`, `build_collaboration_workflows()`, and `COLLABORATION_ADVISORY` added to core; all operations are strictly read-only with no agent execution, automatic delegation, API integration, CLI launching, or routing.
- Added Agent Configuration Model (Phase 37E): `pcae agents config show AGENT_ID` and `pcae agents config show AGENT_ID --json` expose governed configuration metadata for any registered agent (agent_id, adapter_type, configuration_status, executable_hint, requires_manual_setup, configuration_notes, lifecycle_status); unknown agent IDs exit 1 with a clear "Agent not found" message; adapter types are cli, api, desktop_manual, native, and undeclared; initial mapping assigns claude-local and codex-local to cli, pcae-native to native, and all five declared future agents to undeclared; configuration_status is "configured" for non-undeclared adapters and "unconfigured" for undeclared; `pcae agents config validate` and `pcae agents config validate --json` validate the configuration model, checking for duplicate IDs, invalid adapter types, and available/active agents using undeclared adapter; output includes agent count, validation status (valid/invalid), errors, warnings, and advisory "Agent configuration metadata is advisory; configuration does not imply execution."; JSON output has fields valid, agent_count, errors, warnings, advisory; exit code is 0 when valid and 1 when errors exist; `AgentConfigEntry`, `AgentConfigValidationResult`, `AGENT_CONFIG_REGISTRY`, `get_agent_config()`, `validate_agent_configs()`, adapter type constants, and `CONFIG_ADVISORY` added to core; all operations are strictly read-only with no agent execution, API integration, CLI launching, automatic routing, or availability probing.
- Added Agent Lifecycle State Management (Phase 37D): `pcae agents lifecycle` and `pcae agents lifecycle --json` report lifecycle state distribution and progression guidance for all registered agents; human-readable output includes agent count, state distribution (active=N, available=N, configured=N, declared=N), agents grouped by lifecycle state showing agent_id, agent_type, and role, lifecycle progression guidance for each of the four states (declared, configured, available, active), and the advisory "Lifecycle reporting is advisory; no agent state is modified."; JSON output includes lifecycle_summary (count per state), agents_by_state (agents grouped by state with full entry metadata), progression_guidance (guidance string per state), validation (valid, errors, warnings), and advisory; validation checks for duplicate agent IDs, invalid lifecycle states, and inconsistent lifecycle metadata (available/active agents without capabilities or preferred workloads); `build_lifecycle_report()`, `_validate_lifecycle()`, `LifecycleReport`, `LifecycleValidationResult`, `LIFECYCLE_ADVISORY`, and `LIFECYCLE_PROGRESSION_GUIDANCE` added to core; all operations are strictly read-only with no agent execution, API integration, CLI launching, automatic routing, availability probing, or state modification.
- Added Agent Configuration and Availability Governance (Phase 37C): `pcae agents show AGENT_ID` and `pcae agents show AGENT_ID --json` display full metadata (agent_id, agent_type, role, status, capabilities, preferred_workloads) for any registered agent; unknown agent IDs exit 1 with "Agent not found: '<id>'."; `pcae agents validate` and `pcae agents validate --json` validate registry consistency with four checks — duplicate IDs, invalid lifecycle statuses, non-empty roles, and available/active agents having capabilities and preferred workloads; output includes agent count, validation status (valid/invalid), errors list, warnings list, and advisory "Agent configuration validation is advisory; the user remains authoritative."; JSON output has fields valid, agent_count, errors, warnings, advisory; exit code is 0 when valid and 1 when errors exist; `get_agent_by_id()`, `validate_agent_registry()`, and `AgentValidationResult` added to core; `AGENT_VALIDATION_ADVISORY` constant exported; all operations are read-only with no agent execution, API integration, CLI launching, automatic routing, or availability probing.
- Added Multi-Agent Registry Expansion and Lifecycle States (Phase 37B): the agent registry expands from 3 to 8 entries; four lifecycle statuses are introduced — declared, configured, available, active — validated on `AgentEntry` construction via `__post_init__` so invalid statuses raise `ValueError`; `VALID_AGENT_STATUSES` and four `AGENT_STATUS_*` constants are exported; three existing agents (claude-local, codex-local, pcae-native) remain `available`; five new vendor-neutral agents (kimi-local/kimi/analysis, deepseek-local/deepseek/implementation, gemini-local/gemini/analysis, grok-local/grok/analysis, perplexity-local/perplexity/research) are added as `declared`, indicating they are registered but not configured or confirmed for local use; `pcae agents` human output shows all eight agents with lifecycle status and a "Lifecycle summary: available=3, declared=5" line; `pcae agents --json` output gains a `lifecycle_summary` object with per-status counts (active, available, configured, declared); `build_multi_agent_registry()` includes `lifecycle_summary`; declared agents are not executable, available, or remotely reachable; no API integration, CLI launching, automatic routing, or availability probing; design remains vendor-neutral and advisory.
- Added Multi-Agent Collaboration Foundation (Phase 37A): `pcae agents` and `pcae agents --json` inspect the built-in multi-agent registry; each entry carries agent_id, agent_type, role, status, capabilities, and preferred_workloads; initial agents are claude-local (claude/documentation), codex-local (codex/implementation), and pcae-native (pcae/governance); human output reports agent count, agent id, role, and status; JSON output includes a full agents list with capability summaries and the advisory "Agent registry is read-only. The human user remains authoritative."; the roadmap transitions from Option B — Architecture Memory to Option C — Multi-Agent Collaboration with next recommended phase 37B Multi-Agent Capability Registry; `pcae roadmap next` now recommends Phase 37B and cites Option C; PREDICTED_PHASES_OPTION_C is introduced alongside the completed PREDICTED_PHASES_OPTION_B; PROJECT_STATUS.md current phase updated to Phase 37A; the registry is fully read-only, vendor-neutral, and does not perform automatic delegation, task routing, collaboration workflows, or remote execution.
- Started PCAE Harness project.
- Added `pcae roadmap next` and `pcae roadmap next --json` for deterministic, read-only governed roadmap recommendations based on governance audit, health, active task, TODO/DONE, project status, continuity, and orchestration readiness signals. Recommendations are advisory only and preserve human authority without creating tasks, modifying artifacts, or mutating runtime state.
- Added `pcae orchestration select TASK_TYPE` and `pcae orchestration select TASK_TYPE --json` for deterministic, advisory agent selection using the current orchestration policy and agent registry. Selection reuses the existing recommendation logic, reports matched role and fallback status, and does not mutate locks or runtime state.
- Added `pcae orchestration explain TASK_TYPE` and `pcae orchestration explain TASK_TYPE --json` for advisory explanations of agent recommendations, including matched role, fallback behavior, and alternative registered agents with why-not-selected notes. The command is read-only and does not mutate locks or runtime state.
- Added Architecture memory session restore command (Phase 36N): `pcae architecture restore-session` and `pcae architecture restore-session --json` generate a compact read-only architecture memory restore summary for fresh AI sessions; output includes decision_count, accepted_count, latest_decision (id, title, status, author, phase_reference, is_human_approved), linkage_summary (commit_reference, provenance_reference, contributors deduplicated across the registry, is_human_approved), session_guidance (decision counts including proposed, advisory notes, inspection commands), and advisory "Architecture memory restore is advisory; no ADRs are modified."; proposed decisions are surfaced in session guidance when present; the command is fully read-only and does not mutate ADRs, continuity packs, or any files.
- Added Architecture governance audit integration (Phase 36M): `pcae governance audit` now includes an `architecture_memory` check that verifies the ADR registry is readable, passes validation (no duplicate IDs or unknown statuses), and has no unparseable persisted ADR files; `GovernanceAuditResult` gains an `architecture_memory_summary` field (decision_count, accepted_count, latest_decision, warnings, errors); `pcae governance audit --json` includes `architecture_memory_summary` in output; `pcae governance audit` human output displays an "Architecture memory summary" section; malformed `.pcae/architecture/*.json` files cause the check to fail with a clear error; the `architecture_memory` check name is registered in `_GOVERNANCE_AUDIT_KNOWN_CHECKS`; a `count_adr_parse_failures(root)` helper is added to detect silently-skipped ADR files; all operations are read-only and do not mutate ADRs.
- Added Architecture Memory continuity integration (Phase 36L): `ContextPack` gains an `architecture_memory` field with compact summary (decision_count, accepted_count, latest_decision, advisory); `build_context_pack` populates it from the live ADR registry; `build_bootstrap_prompt` includes a single compact "Architecture memory: N decisions (M accepted), latest: ADR-XXXX" line; `ContinuityPack` includes `architecture_memory` in its JSON export; `pcae context pack --preview` displays an "Architecture memory" section; `pcae context pack --preview --json` includes `architecture_memory` in output; `pcae continuity export --json` includes `architecture_memory_present` in `continuity_summary`; `pcae continuity inspect` reports `Architecture memory present:`; `pcae continuity inspect --json` includes `architecture_memory_present` in continuity_summary; a new "architecture memory" is added to `CONTINUITY_PACK_INCLUDED_SECTIONS`; `pcae continuity compatibility` includes an `architecture_memory_presence` check (advisory; absent packs remain compatible); `architecture_memory` is treated as a known optional key and excluded from future-version warnings; full ADR bodies are not included in context or bootstrap output.
- Added Architecture provenance linkage to governed Architecture Decision Records (Phase 36K): `ArchitectureDecisionRecord` gains two optional fields (`commit_reference`, `provenance_reference`) captured at creation time when available; `add_architecture_decision` records the short HEAD commit SHA via `git rev-parse --short HEAD` and the timestamp of the latest provenance event; existing ADRs without these fields load with `None` and remain valid; `pcae architecture show DECISION_ID` displays an "Architecture linkage" section (Phase, Commit, Provenance, Contributors, Human approved) and `--json` output includes an `architecture_linkage` object; `pcae architecture decisions --json` includes `architecture_linkage` in each decision; all operations remain read-only for inspection; `build_architecture_linkage(adr)` returns "unavailable" for absent fields.
- Added governed Architecture Decision Record status validation command (Phase 36J): `pcae architecture validate` and `pcae architecture validate --json` validate the full ADR registry (sample + persisted) for status integrity issues; checks include duplicate decision IDs and unknown statuses; `valid` flag is True when no issues are found; exit code 0 = valid, 1 = issues found; the command is read-only and does not mutate any ADR or artifact; advisory included in all output.
- Added governed Architecture Decision Record export command (Phase 36I): `pcae architecture export` and `pcae architecture export --json` export all ADRs (sample + persisted) to `.pcae/architecture-exports/architecture-decisions-YYYYMMDD-HHMMSS.json`; the export bundle includes `exported_at`, `decision_count`, `decisions` (all ten ADR fields plus `is_human_approved`), `statuses` (per-status count for all four valid statuses), and `advisory`; export files are Git-ignored via `.pcae/.gitignore`; command is read-only and does not mutate persisted ADRs.
- Added governed Architecture Decision Record creation command (Phase 36H): `pcae architecture add --title TEXT --rationale TEXT --author TEXT` creates a new ADR using the existing model and persists it as JSON under `.pcae/architecture/ADR-YYYYMMDD-HHMMSS.json`; decision IDs are generated sequentially (ADR-0003, ADR-0004, ...) combining the sample registry and any already-persisted ADRs; `--status TEXT` defaults to `accepted`; `--alternative`, `--consequence`, and `--contributor` are repeatable; `--phase-reference TEXT` is optional; invalid statuses exit 1 with a clear error; `pcae architecture decisions` and `pcae architecture show` now include persisted ADRs from `.pcae/architecture/`; persisted ADR files are Git-ignored via `.pcae/.gitignore`; human author is required; contributors are vendor-neutral string identifiers.
- Added governed Architecture Decision Record inspection commands (Phase 36G): `pcae architecture decisions` and `pcae architecture decisions --json` list all ADRs with id, title, status, and phase reference; `pcae architecture show DECISION_ID` and `pcae architecture show DECISION_ID --json` show full ADR detail including all ten fields and `is_human_approved`; unknown decision IDs exit 1 with a clear "not found" message; a deterministic in-memory sample registry (ADR-0001, ADR-0002) provides stable fixture data until Phase 36H; all output includes the advisory "Architecture decision inspection is advisory; the user remains authoritative."; commands are read-only and do not mutate any artifacts.
- Added governed Architecture Decision Record (ADR) model (Phase 36F): `ArchitectureDecisionRecord` dataclass with ten fields (decision_id, title, status, rationale, alternatives_considered, consequences, created_at, phase_reference, author, contributors) and `create_adr()` factory; four lifecycle statuses: proposed, accepted, superseded, deprecated; `is_human_approved` property is True only when status is "accepted"; `create_adr()` raises ValueError for unknown statuses or empty required fields; human author is required (human remains authoritative); contributors field is vendor-neutral and accepts any string identifiers including AI agent IDs; no CLI commands, persistence, export, or automatic decision generation in this phase.
- Added roadmap awareness for predicted phases (Phase 36E): `pcae roadmap next` and `pcae roadmap next --json` now reference the agreed strategic roadmap sequence (Option B — Architecture Memory → Option C — Multi-Agent Collaboration → Remote Coding) and predicted phases for Option B (36F–36M) when no pending TODO items exist; `roadmap_sequence` and `predicted_phases` are included in JSON output; when TODO items exist, the first TODO is recommended and `predicted_phases` is empty; recommendations remain advisory, no tasks are created automatically, and no runtime state is mutated.
- Added `pcae orchestration capabilities` and `pcae orchestration capabilities --json` to expose the governed agent capability matrix from the current policy-declared registry. The command lists agents, kinds, and roles, remains advisory, and does not assign work or mutate runtime state.

Reports active task (id/title), governance state (health status, check status, session continuity, agent lock state), orchestration state (policy summary, registered agents, default agent), provenance summary (event count, latest event), roadmap summary (current phase and next items parsed from PROJECT_STATUS.md), fixed operational rules (phase prompt authority, PROJECT_STATUS.md is background context, do not infer stale tasks, active task scope, always run pcae check and tests), validation commands (pcae health, pcae check, python -m pytest, git status), and the quality preservation advisory that the pack reduces context size but does not relax governance constraints. Does not write files, mutate runtime state, or weaken governance.
- Extended `pcae context pack --preview` and `pcae context pack --preview --json` with universal compact context quality improvements: scope boundaries (allowed and forbidden files parsed from the active task contract), bootstrap/handoff notes (`pcae session bootstrap --agent-id <id>` for fresh sessions, `pcae phase handoff` for agent transitions), orchestration advisory recommendation semantics (advisory recommendations are non-binding; the human user remains authoritative), universal agent note (vendor-neutral; not tailored to any specific AI agent or provider), and stale-context suppression rules. JSON output now includes `scope_boundaries` (allowed_files and forbidden_files lists) and `bootstrap_handoff_notes` (list of bootstrap and handoff instructions). Orchestration state now includes `advisory_recommendation_semantics`. Quality preservation note updated to "Optimization reduces context size without relaxing governance constraints."
- Added optional `--profile` flag to `pcae context pack --preview` for work-mode governed context profiles: `implementation` (emphasizes active task scope, allowed files, validation commands, roadmap, operational constraints), `documentation` (emphasizes roadmap, architecture/governance semantics, operational rules), `validation` (emphasizes health/check state, validation commands, provenance summary), and `handoff` (emphasizes session continuity, agent lock, provenance, bootstrap/handoff guidance, orchestration state). Unknown profiles fall back to the balanced universal profile with a clear warning. All profiles preserve governance safety, operational rules, validation expectations, phase prompt authority, active task boundaries, and vendor neutrality. JSON output includes `profile_type` and `emphasized_sections`; unknown profiles include `profile_warning`. Profiles optimize by work mode, not by vendor or model.
- Added `pcae session bootstrap --compact` for read-only compact governed bootstrap prompt generation. `--compact` mode builds on the context pack and work-mode profile system to produce a structured, token-efficient prompt suitable for fresh AI sessions, post-auto-compact recovery, cross-agent handoff, and token-efficient continuity restoration. The prompt includes active task, governance state (health/check/session/lock), current phase, profile emphasis, operational rules, validation commands, stale-context suppression, bootstrap/handoff guidance, orchestration advisory semantics, and a vendor-neutral note. Supports `--profile` for work-mode emphasis and `--json` for machine-readable output (fields: `advisory`, `bootstrap_prompt`, `governance_state`, `operational_rules`, `orchestration_state`, `profile_type`, `validation_commands`). Read-only: does not acquire locks, append provenance events, or mutate any governance state. Made `--agent-id` optional at the CLI level (validated in the handler when `--compact` is absent). Advisory: "Bootstrap compression reduces token usage without relaxing governance constraints."
- Added `pcae context export` to export a compact governed context pack as an ignored local artifact under `.pcae/context-packs/` (filename `context-pack-YYYYMMDD-HHMMSS.txt`). Reuses `build_bootstrap_prompt` content (compact bootstrap format). Supports `--profile` for work-mode emphasis and `--json` for machine-readable output (fields: `path`, `profile_type`, `exported_at`). Exported files are ignored by Git via `context-packs/` entry in `.pcae/.gitignore`. Does not inject prompts, sync remotely, or mutate governance state.
- Added `pcae continuity export` to export a portable governed continuity restore pack as an ignored JSON artifact under `.pcae/continuity-packs/` (filename `continuity-pack-YYYYMMDD-HHMMSS.json`). Combines runtime snapshot metadata, compact context pack, compact bootstrap prompt, active task summary, governance state, orchestration state, provenance summary, operational rules, validation commands, stale-context suppression rules, bootstrap continuity notes, and a vendor-neutral note. Supports `--profile` for work-mode emphasis and `--json` for machine-readable output (fields: `path`, `profile_type`, `exported_at`, `included_sections`, `continuity_summary`). Exported packs are ignored by Git via `continuity-packs/` entry in `.pcae/.gitignore`. Continuity packs are governance-complete, vendor-neutral, portable, and read-only exports: no automatic restore, prompt injection, remote sync, telemetry, or runtime mutation.
- Added `pcae continuity inspect PATH` to inspect exported continuity packs read-only.
