Supports `--json` for machine-readable output (fields: `valid`, `exported_at`, `profile_type`, `included_sections`, `continuity_summary`, `portability_notes`, `safety_notes`, `advisory`). Raises a clear error for missing files, invalid JSON, non-object JSON, or missing required fields. Does not restore runtime state, mutate continuity packs, or modify governance artifacts.
- Added `pcae continuity compatibility PATH` to analyze compatibility of exported continuity packs against the current PCAE runtime. Runs nine checks: structure validity, required sections presence, governance state presence, compact bootstrap presence, operational rules presence, stale-context suppression presence, vendor-neutral note presence, runtime snapshot metadata compatibility, and future-version warning support. Reports support level (`supported`, `partially-supported`, `unsupported`), per-check pass/warn status, deduplicated warnings, governance continuity summary, portability summary, and the advisory "Continuity compatibility analysis is advisory; no runtime state is changed." Supports `--json` for machine-readable output (fields: `compatible`, `support_level`, `compatibility_checks`, `warnings`, `continuity_summary`, `advisory`). Raises a clear error for missing files, invalid JSON, or non-object JSON. Does not mutate continuity packs, restore runtime state, or modify governance artifacts.
- Added `pcae continuity manifest` to index exported continuity packs deterministically. Scans `.pcae/continuity-packs/` and returns pack count, latest pack, manifest entries sorted newest-first by exported_at, and compatibility summary counts (compatible/incompatible/supported/partially-supported/unsupported). Each manifest entry includes filename, exported_at, profile_type, governance_health, governance_check, active_task_id, compatibility_status, support_level, vendor_neutral, stale_context_suppression_present, and compact_bootstrap_present. Supports `--json` for machine-readable output (fields: `pack_count`, `latest_pack`, `manifest_entries`, `compatibility_summary`, `advisory`). Advisory: "Continuity manifests are advisory; the user remains authoritative." Does not mutate continuity packs, prune packs, restore runtime state, or modify governance artifacts.
- Added Phase 44C.1 documentation capability discovery: augments `pcae capability-discovery` with a static `_DOC_CAPABILITY_CATALOG` mapping agent_id → vendor-documented capabilities. Catalog entries: codex-local (subagent-coordination, skill-execution), claude-local (subagent-coordination, custom-agent-support), kimi-local (swarm-coordination). Documentation evidence produces at most `observed` confidence — never `validated` or `proven`. Added `"custom-agent-support"` to `CAPABILITY_CATEGORIES` (20 categories total). Discovery merges documentation evidence with CLI and runtime discovery: if a capability is already known (e.g. claude's subagent-coordination from CLI help), `documentation_reference` is appended to its existing evidence_sources without downgrading confidence; if unknown, a new `observed` entry is created. Documentation applies regardless of installation status. Future agents without catalog entries remain `unknown` and do not fail discovery. New evidence source label: `documentation_reference`. 10 new tests verifying per-agent doc promotion, max-observed constraint, multi-source accumulation, and future-agent isolation.
- Fixed Phase 44C capability auto-discovery: `subagent_capable_agents` was always empty because `_KW_CAP_SUBAGENT` only matched `("subagent", "sub-agent", "agent team")` — none of which appear in real CLI help texts. Expanded `_KW_CAP_SUBAGENT` (and the shared `_KW_SUBAGENTS` used by runtime discovery) to include `"background agent"` (matches Claude's "Manage background agents"), `"multi-agent"` (matches Claude's ultrareview command), and `"--agents"` (matches Claude's `--agents <json>` option). These keywords are vendor-neutral: any future CLI that uses the same terminology will be detected without code changes. Also integrated `build_runtime_discovery()` as a formal secondary evidence source in `build_capability_discovery()` — the runtime discovery result is passed into each per-agent profile build and contributes a `runtime_discovery` evidence source when `subagents_supported == "yes"`. Also made subcommand probing executable-agnostic (probes `exec`, `mcp`, `mcp-server` for any executable, not just codex). With these changes, `claude-local` is correctly detected as subagent-capable with confidence `observed` and evidence sources `["CLI help inspection", "runtime_discovery"]`. Added 4 new mechanism-level tests that verify: `subagent_capable_agents` is consistent with per-agent `subagent_profile.supported`; only approved evidence sources are cited; installed agents with subagent support report `observed` (not `unknown`); and CLI/runtime discovery is always in the evidence chain for observed subagent capabilities.
- Added `pcae capability-registry`, `pcae capability-registry --json`, `pcae capability-discovery`, and `pcae capability-discovery --json` (Phase 44C) for evidence-based agent capability auto-discovery. `capability-registry` shows the static capability registry (adapter contracts + execution history, no CLI probing); `capability-discovery` runs full auto-discovery (CLI help inspection + execution history + adapter contracts). Both cover 7 agents (codex-local, claude-local, kimi-local, deepseek-local, gemini-local, grok-local, perplexity-local) and 19 capability categories (planning, implementation, review, validation, research, testing, architecture, documentation, security, performance, dependency-analysis, data-science, devops, refactoring, code-generation, roadmap-generation, subagent-coordination, skill-execution, swarm-coordination). Per-agent profile includes agent_id, runtime, lifecycle_status, installed, version, capabilities (with name/confidence/evidence_sources/notes), and subagent_profile (supported/confidence/mechanism/evidence_sources/notes). Confidence levels: unknown → observed → validated → proven. Evidence sources: adapter_contract, manual_validation, runtime_discovery, CLI help inspection, governed_execution_history, writable_execution_history, documentation_reference. Discovery rules: subagent/skill/swarm capabilities are at most `observed` from CLI help (never proven); declared agents with no installation remain `unknown`; writable execution history promotes `implementation` to `proven`; governed execution history promotes code-generation/testing/validation to `proven`. JSON output: `capability_registry`, `discovery_summary`, `advisory`. Read-only: no agents executed, no prompts submitted. Advisory: "Capability registry is advisory; capabilities are evidence-based and should be refreshed after runtime updates." 24 new tests.
- Added `pcae orchestration-design` and `pcae orchestration-design --json` (Phase 44B) for read-only multi-agent orchestration architecture design. Covers: coordinator responsibilities (task_decomposition, role_assignment, parallel_execution_planning, result_collection, conflict_detection, consensus_calculation, governance_handoff); capability profile model (fields: agent_id, runtime, lifecycle_status, capabilities, writable_supported, subagent_supported, evidence_source, confidence; 13 capability categories: planning, implementation, review, validation, research, testing, architecture, documentation, security, performance, dependency-analysis, data-science, devops); five orchestration patterns (sequential, parallel_review, parallel_planning, swarm, full_pipeline); governance integration rules (only implementer may modify files; planner/reviewer/validator read-only by default; file modification requires existing governance; commit/push separately governed; human remains authoritative); conflict resolution policies (unanimous, majority, weighted, human_escalation; default: human_escalation); and future agent expansion (deepseek-local, gemini-local, grok-local, perplexity-local, future cloud/local agents). JSON output includes `orchestration_design`, `capability_profile_model`, `orchestration_patterns`, `governance_integration`, `conflict_resolution`, `future_agent_expansion`, and `advisory`. Strictly read-only — no orchestration executed, no agents spawned, no files modified. Advisory: "Multi-agent orchestration design is advisory; no orchestration is performed." 13 new tests.
- Added `pcae continuity retention --dry-run` and `pcae continuity retention --dry-run --json` for read-only retention planning that keeps the latest five continuity packs and marks older packs as prune candidates without deleting anything. Human-readable output reports pack count, keep count, prune candidate count, packs to keep, and prune candidates. JSON output includes `pack_count`, `keep_count`, `prune_candidate_count`, `keep`, `prune_candidates`, and `advisory`. Advisory: "Continuity retention planning is advisory; no continuity packs are deleted." Does not delete continuity packs, mutate continuity packs, restore runtime state, or modify governance artifacts.
- Added `pcae governance sync-check` and `pcae governance sync-check --json` for read-only governance artifact synchronization validation. Analyzes PROJECT_STATUS.md, tasks/TODO.md, CHANGELOG.md, and tasks/DONE.md to detect stale references (known completed features still listed as pending), completed TODO entries (pending items whose `pcae` commands appear in DONE.md or CHANGELOG.md), inconsistent roadmap entries (Next items whose commands appear in DONE.md), and governance audit capability gaps (checks absent from `pcae governance audit` — specifically `artifact_sync_drift`). Human-readable output reports synchronization status, stale references, completed TODO entries, inconsistent roadmap entries, and governance drift warnings. JSON output includes `synchronized`, `stale_references`, `completed_todo_entries`, `inconsistent_entries`, `governance_drift_warnings`, and `advisory`. Advisory: "Synchronization analysis is advisory; no governance artifacts are modified." Does not mutate artifacts, auto-repair TODO.md, rewrite PROJECT_STATUS.md, or modify CHANGELOG.md.
- Integrated `artifact_sync_drift` check into `pcae governance audit` and `pcae governance audit --json`. The new check runs `check_governance_sync` internally and passes when governance artifacts are synchronized or when drift issues are present (drift surfaces as warnings, not failures). Drift warnings from `find_artifact_sync_drift_warnings` report completed TODO entries still listed as pending and inconsistent roadmap entries; stale references continue to be reported by the existing `find_stale_roadmap_references` path without double-counting. Adding `artifact_sync_drift` to `_GOVERNANCE_AUDIT_KNOWN_CHECKS` closes the gap that `pcae governance sync-check` previously reported as a drift warning. The audit remains read-only: no artifacts are mutated, no TODO entries are removed, and no roadmap files are rewritten.
- Added `pcae governance sync-repair --dry-run` and `pcae governance sync-repair --dry-run --json` for deterministic read-only repair previews for stale governance artifacts with artifact-type-aware semantics: operational artifacts (tasks/TODO.md, PROJECT_STATUS.md) propose remove or update actions; historical artifacts (CHANGELOG.md, tasks/DONE.md) propose preserve actions and are never proposed for removal. Reuses existing `check_governance_sync` logic to generate per-repair entries for: completed TODO entries still pending (action: remove, artifact: tasks/TODO.md), stale roadmap/command references across governance artifacts (action: remove, per-artifact), inconsistent roadmap entries whose commands appear in DONE.md (action: remove, artifact: PROJECT_STATUS.md), and governance audit capability gaps (action: update, artifact: governance audit). Each repair entry includes the target artifact, stale entry, proposed action (remove/update/relocate), and rationale. Human-readable output shows "Governance synchronization repair preview", proposed repairs with artifact/stale_entry/action/rationale fields, and the advisory note "Repair preview is advisory; no governance artifacts are modified." JSON output includes `repairable`, `proposed_repairs` (list of artifact/stale_entry/action/rationale objects), and `advisory`. Does not modify governance artifacts, auto-repair TODO.md, rewrite CHANGELOG.md, or mutate runtime state.
- Added `pcae governance artifacts` and `pcae governance artifacts --json` to expose the governance artifact classification registry as a reusable read-only command (Phase 35S). Lists all 10 known governance artifacts grouped by class: operational (PROJECT_STATUS.md, tasks/TODO.md — repair: actionable, source control: tracked), historical (CHANGELOG.md, tasks/DONE.md — repair: preserve, source control: tracked), runtime (.pcae/provenance-history.json, .pcae/agent-lock.json, .pcae/session.json — repair: ignore, source control: ignored), and generated (.pcae/runtime-snapshots/**, .pcae/context-packs/**, .pcae/continuity-packs/** — repair: ignore, source control: generated_ignored). Human-readable output groups entries by class with repair policy label and source control role. JSON output includes `artifacts` (list of path, artifact_class, governance_role, repair_policy, source_control_role per entry), `classes` (ordered list of artifact classes), and `advisory`. Registry reuses `classify_governance_artifact` from Phase 35R. Does not mutate artifacts, modify source control, or change sync-check/sync-repair behavior. Advisory: "Artifact classification is advisory; the user remains authoritative."
- Added `pcae governance artifacts export` and `pcae governance artifacts export --json` for exporting the governance artifact classification registry as a portable ignored artifact (Phase 35U). Exports to `.pcae/governance-exports/artifact-registry-YYYYMMDD-HHMMSS.json`. Export file includes: `exported_at`, `exported_by_version`, `artifact_count`, `classes`, `artifacts` (with path, artifact_class, governance_role, repair_policy, and source_control_role per entry), and `advisory`. Human-readable output reports export path, artifact count, classes, and exported_at timestamp. JSON output includes export_path, exported_at, artifact_count, classes, and advisory. Added `.pcae/governance-exports/` to `.pcae/.gitignore` so export files are ignored by Git. Added `.pcae/governance-exports/**` to `GOVERNANCE_ARTIFACT_REGISTRY` and `_GENERATED_ARTIFACT_PREFIXES` so the classifier correctly recognizes export files as generated artifacts. Does not mutate governance artifacts, repair anything, or modify source control. Export-only command; registry import, automatic repair, and semantic analysis are not implemented.
- Added `pcae governance registry-audit` and `pcae governance registry-audit --json` for read-only audit of governance registry consumer coverage (Phase 35T). Reports whether key governance systems are registry-backed: sync-check (uses `classify_governance_artifact` via `_artifact_type_for`), sync-repair (uses `classify_governance_artifact` via `_artifact_type_for` and `_stale_ref_proposed_action`), governance audit (uses `classify_governance_artifact` via artifact_sync_drift check), and artifact registry (uses `GOVERNANCE_ARTIFACT_REGISTRY` directly). Human-readable output reports registry audit status, consumers checked with registry-backed status and note per consumer, warnings (none if all consumers are registry-backed), and advisory "Registry audit is advisory; no governance artifacts are modified." JSON output includes `registry_audit_status`, `consumers` (list of name/registry_backed/note per consumer), `warnings`, and `advisory`. Command is read-only: does not mutate artifacts, rewrite governance files, scan source beyond deterministic helpers, or modify any runtime state.
- Centralized governance artifact lifecycle classification in `classify_governance_artifact` and `ArtifactClassification` (Phase 35R). Replaces implicit `_HISTORICAL_ARTIFACTS` frozenset with a deterministic four-class registry: operational (PROJECT_STATUS.md, tasks/TODO.md — live guidance, actionable drift candidates), historical (CHANGELOG.md, tasks/DONE.md — preserved records, never proposed for removal), runtime (.pcae/provenance-history.json, .pcae/agent-lock.json, .pcae/session.json — runtime governance state, ignored for source repair), and generated (.pcae/runtime-snapshots/**, .pcae/context-packs/**, .pcae/continuity-packs/** — generated artifacts, ignored for source repair). `classify_governance_artifact(artifact)` returns an `ArtifactClassification` with `artifact_type`, `artifact_class`, and `governance_role`. `pcae governance sync-check` and `pcae governance sync-repair` now use the classifier for operational vs. historical vs. runtime vs. generated semantics. `SyncRepairEntry.to_dict()` now exposes `artifact_class` and `governance_role` in JSON output. Human-readable repair preview output now explicitly states that runtime and generated artifacts (.pcae/**) are ignored for source governance repair. Current behavior is preserved: operational artifacts remain actionable, historical artifacts remain preserved. Classifier is deterministic and read-only; no artifacts are modified.
